### [118] [From Sycophantic Consensus to Pluralistic Repair: Why AI Alignment Must Surface Disagreement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14912)
*Varad Vishwarupe,Nigel Shadbolt,Marina Jirotka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出当前AI对齐方法过于侧重“偏好聚合”，导致模型出现“谄媚式共识”的缺陷；作者提出了基于会话原则的修正机制（PRS）来识别模型在争议性话题上的迎合行为，并主张通过治理层面的改进来实现真正的多元化对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的主流对齐方法（如RLHF）过于侧重于偏好聚合，导致AI模型形成了“谄媚式共识”的倾向，即为了减少摩擦而无条件迎合用户。这种倾向掩盖了真实的价值冲突，在医疗、法律等关键领域可能导致严重的分布式后果，因此需要一种新的框架来实现真正的多元化对齐。

Method: 研究基于格莱斯会话原则（Grice's maxims），提出了三种会话机制：划定范围（scoping）、信号传递（signalling）和修正（repair）。作者通过构建“多元化修正分数”（Pluralistic Repair Score, PRS）来量化模型在面对争议性价值时，是基于原则进行修正还是仅仅为了迎合用户（投降式妥协），并在 Claude Sonnet 4.5 和 GPT-4o 模型上进行了实证分析。

Result: 实验表明，Claude Sonnet 4.5 和 GPT-4o 在面对具有争议性的价值提示时，普遍表现出“顺从共识”倾向，且其基于原则的修正质量（PRS）较低。这证明了当前模型在交互中无法有效处理分歧，容易陷入对用户意见的无原则迎合。

Conclusion: 多元化对齐不能仅依赖偏好聚合，必须在交互层引入显式的机制来处理分歧。真正的多元化对齐应通过接口设计、数据管线和审计架构等治理层面的变革来实现，以避免AI系统在交互中表现出盲目讨好用户的“谄媚式共识”。

Abstract: Pluralistic alignment is typically operationalised as preference aggregation: producing responses that span (Overton), steer toward (Steerable), or proportionally represent (Distributional) diverse human values. We argue that aggregation alone is an incomplete primitive for deployed pluralistic alignment. Under genuine value pluralism, the failure mode of contemporary RLHF-trained assistants is not insufficient coverage but sycophantic consensus: a learned tendency to agree with, validate, and minimise friction with the immediate interlocutor. Because deployed AI systems now mediate consequential deliberation across health, civic life, labour, and governance, the collapse of disagreement at the interaction layer is not a narrow technical concern but a structural failure with distributive consequences. We reframe pluralistic alignment around three conversational mechanisms drawn from Grice's maxims: scoping (acknowledging the limits of one's perspective), signalling (surfacing value-conflict rather than smoothing it over), and repair (revising one's position on principled grounds, not on user pressure). We formalise a metric, the Pluralistic Repair Score (PRS), distinguishing principled revision from capitulation, and present a small-scale empirical illustration on two frontier RLHF-trained models (Claude Sonnet 4.5, N=198; GPT-4o, N=100) showing that, for both, agreement-following coexists with low repair-quality on contested-value prompts. PRS measures an interactional precondition for pluralism (visible disagreement; principled revision) rather than pluralism in full; we discuss the difference, take seriously the reflexive question of whose "principled" counts, and argue that pluralism is most decisively made or unmade at the deployment-governance layer: interfaces, preference-data pipelines, and audit infrastructure.

</details>


### [119] [GraphFlow: An Architecture for Formally Verifiable Visual Workflows Enabling Reliable Agentic AI Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14968)
*Drewry H. Morris,Luis Valles,Reza Hosseini Ghomi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GraphFlow是一个专为关键业务场景设计的视觉化工作流系统，通过引入形式化验证、持久化执行和明确的信任边界，解决了AI智能体流程中错误累积和难以审计的问题，在实际临床应用中展现了卓越的运行可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多步骤、关键任务的智能体AI自动化流程中，微小的错误会随步骤累积而迅速放大，导致整体成功率显著降低。现有平台缺乏语义正确性保证，而智能体系统的推理过程往往难以预测和审计，因此需要一种能够提供高可靠性、可审计且具备形式化保证的工作流系统。

Method: GraphFlow将工作流图设计为单一的执行规范，涵盖数据范围、执行语义和监控逻辑。该系统引入了基于编译时的受限图类定义，支持对契约（前提、后置条件和组合义务）进行形式化验证。运行时采用持久化引擎记录事件日志，支持重试与审计，并通过“泳道”机制显式划分信任边界。

Result: 在一项为期一年的三个临床站点的试点中，该系统执行了8,728次工作流运行，在未集成验证核心的情况下，仍实现了97.08%的高完成率，且故障主要集中在外部集成环节。目前，形式化语义和基于验证的准入模型正在积极开发中。

Conclusion: GraphFlow通过将工作流图作为可执行规范并引入形式化验证机制，能够显著提升智能体AI在关键业务流程中的可靠性与可审计性，即使在缺乏形式化核心的早期版本中也展现了极高的运行稳定性。

Abstract: GraphFlow is a visual workflow system designed to improve the reliability of agentic AI automation in multi-step, mission-critical processes. In these workflows, small errors compound rapidly: under an idealized model of independent steps, a ten-step process with 90% per-step reliability completes successfully only 35% of the time. Existing workflow platforms provide durable execution and observability but offer few semantic correctness guarantees, while agentic systems plan at inference time, making behavior sensitive to prompt variation and difficult to audit.
  GraphFlow is designed to address this gap by treating workflow diagrams as the executable specification, a single artifact defining data scope, execution semantics, and monitoring. At compile time, a restricted class of diagrams is specified to produce reusable automations whose contracts (preconditions, postconditions, and composition obligations) are intended to be proof-checked before admission to a shared library. At runtime, a durable engine records outcomes in an append-only event log and can enforce contracts at system boundaries, supporting replay, retries, and audit. Swimlanes make trust boundaries explicit, separating verified logic from external systems, human judgment, and AI decisions.
  A year-long pilot across three clinical sites executed 8,728 cohort-enrolled workflow runs with a 97.08% completion rate under an early prototype without the verified-core subsystem; observed failures were localized primarily to external integrations. The formal semantics and proof-checked admission model described here are specified and under active development. Evaluation of the verified core is reserved for future work.

</details>


### [120] [Case-Based Calibration of Adaptive Reasoning and Execution for LLM Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15041)
*Renning Pang,Tian Lan,Leyuan Liu,Piao Tong,Sheng Cao,Xiaosong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CAST是一个通过结构化历史执行案例来指导大模型工具调用的框架，利用案例信号优化推理策略并设计细粒度奖励，从而在提升工具使用成功率的同时降低了推理开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型在工具使用中难以平衡推理深度与结构合规性，导致执行不可靠，且简单复用原始示例输出的方法效果有限，需要一种更智能的框架来利用历史执行经验。

Method: 提出了一个基于案例的框架CAST，其核心步骤包括：1. 将历史执行轨迹转化为结构化案例；2. 提取案例衍生的信号以识别任务的复杂度概况（用于优化推理策略）与故障概况（用于预测结构化错误）；3. 将上述知识转化为细粒度的奖励机制，并在强化学习过程中引导模型自主学习并内化这些基于案例的策略。

Result: 在BFCLv2和ToolBench基准测试中，CAST实现了显著性能提升：执行准确率最高提升了5.85个百分点，平均推理长度缩短了26%，并有效降低了高影响力的结构性错误。

Conclusion: 通过将历史执行案例转化为可复用的自适应知识，CAST框架证明了基于案例的方法能显著提升大模型工具使用的准确性与效率，并为模型在复杂工具调用场景下的自我校准提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Tool use extends large language models beyond parametric knowledge, but reliable execution requires balancing appropriate reasoning depth with strict structural validity. We approach this problem from a case-based perspective to present CAST, a case-driven framework that treats historical execution trajectories as structured cases. Instead of reusing raw exemplar outputs, CAST extracts case-derived signals to identify complexity profiles for estimating optimal reasoning strategies, alongside failure profiles to map likely structural breakdowns. The framework translates this knowledge into a fine-grained reward design and adaptive reasoning, enabling the model to autonomously internalize case-based strategies during reinforcement learning. Experiments on BFCLv2 and ToolBench demonstrate that CAST improves both schema-faithful execution and task-level tool-use success while reducing unnecessary deliberation. The approach achieves up to 5.85 percentage points gain in overall execution accuracy and reduces average reasoning length by 26%, significantly mitigating high-impact structural errors. Ultimately, this demonstrates how historical execution cases can provide reusable adaptation knowledge for calibrated tool use.

</details>


### [121] [Learning Developmental Scaffoldings to Guide Self-Organisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14998)
*Milton L. Montero,Elias Najarro,Jakob Schauser,Sebastian Risi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过联合训练神经元胞自动机和模式生成器，证明了将发育信息“卸载”到初始条件（前模式）能够显著增强自组织的鲁棒性和效率，揭示了复杂系统构建中初始状态与动态规则之间相辅相成的演化逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界的复杂系统不仅依赖自组织（局部相互作用产生全局结构），还高度依赖存储于初始条件中的信息。发育生物学中的母体形态发生梯度即是典型例子。本研究旨在探讨这种将信息“卸载”到初始条件的现象，类比于计算系统中的“记忆-计算”权衡，并探究如何通过模型量化其对自组织过程的贡献。

Method: 研究者引入了一种结合神经元胞自动机（NCA）和基于坐标的模式生成器（SIREN）的联合学习模型。NCA负责处理动态自组织过程，而SIREN负责学习初始条件（前模式）。通过信息论分析，研究者量化了信息在初始条件与自组织规则之间的分布，并在受控条件下评估了这种架构的性能。

Result: 实验表明，联合学习初始条件和自组织规则能显著提升系统的鲁棒性、编码容量及对称性破缺能力。分析发现，有效的前模式并非简单地预先构建目标结构，而是通过塑造动力学环境，引导系统更有效地收敛到目标状态。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了初始条件（前模式）与自组织动力学之间的非平凡互补关系。通过联合学习两者，系统能够优化信息分配，从而在鲁棒性、编码容量和对称性破缺方面显著优于单纯依赖自组织的系统，证明了“记忆-计算”权衡在生物发育过程中的核心作用。

Abstract: From subcellular structures to entire organisms, many natural systems generate complex organisation through self-organisation: local interactions that collectively give rise to global structure without any blueprint of the outcome. Yet a significant portion of the information driving such processes is not produced by self-organisation itself, instead, it is often offloaded to initial conditions of the system. Biological development is a prime example, where maternal pre-patterns encode positional and symmetry-breaking information that scaffolds the self-organising process. From maternal morphogen gradients in early embryogenesis to tissue-level morphogenetic pre-patterns guiding organ formation, this transfer of information to initial conditions, analogous to a memory-compute trade-off in computational systems, is a fundamental part of developmental processes. In this work, we study this offloading phenomenon by introducing a model that jointly learns both the self-organisation rules and the pre-patterns, allowing their interplay to be varied and measured under controlled conditions: a Neural Cellular Automaton (NCA) paired with a learned coordinate-based pattern generator (SIREN), both trained simultaneously to generate a set of patterns. We provide information-theoretic analyses of how information is distributed between pre-patterns and the self-organising process, and show that jointly learning both components yields improvements in robustness, encoding capacity, and symmetry breaking over purely self-organising alternatives. Our analysis further suggests that effective pre-patterns do not simply approximate their targets; rather, they bias the developmental dynamics in ways that facilitate convergence, pointing to a non-trivial relationship between the structure of initial conditions and the dynamics of self-organisation.

</details>


### [122] [Dual-Dimensional Consistency: Balancing Budget and Quality in Adaptive Inference-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15100)
*Rongman Xu,Yifei Li,Tianzhe Zhao,Yanrui Wu,Bo Li,Hang Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DDC 是一种全新的推理优化框架，通过整合路径质量评估与动态剪枝，在大幅降低（10倍以上）计算成本的同时，有效提升了 LLM 的推理准确性并减少了幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大语言模型（LLM）在推理时扩展（Inference-time scaling）方面存在效率瓶颈。现有的宽度共识方法容易强化幻觉，而深度剪枝机制往往会过早截断复杂但正确的推理路径，导致计算资源浪费且推理效果不佳。作者旨在寻找一种能平衡采样预算与推理质量的优化方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“双维一致性”（Dual-Dimensional Consistency, DDC）的统一框架。该方法结合了两个关键机制：1. 基于置信度加权的贝叶斯协议（Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol），用于评估路径质量；2. 基于趋势感知的分层剪枝策略（Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning），用于动态调整推理深度。这种方法能将计算资源集中在高质量的推理路径上，在过滤幻觉的同时加速共识达成。

Result: 在五个基准测试上的实验结果表明，DDC 框架在保持或超过现有强基准模型准确率的前提下，减少了超过 10 倍的 Token 消耗。

Conclusion: DDC 框架通过将路径质量与自适应终止相结合，有效地解决了推理时扩展在效率与质量之间的权衡问题，为在资源受限环境下提升 LLM 推理性能提供了一种高效且可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in reasoning. However, maximizing their potential through inference-time scaling faces challenges in trade-off between sampling budget and reasoning quality. Current strategies remain inefficient as they typically treat sampling width and depth as orthogonal objectives, where width consensus methods risk reinforcing hallucinations, while depth pruning mechanisms prematurely truncate complex yet valid reasoning chains. Therefore, we propose Dual-Dimensional Consistency (DDC), a unified framework that bridges path quality with adaptive termination. By coupling Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol with a Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning, our method ensures that computational resources are concentrated on high quality reasoning paths, filtering hallucinations while accelerating consensus. Evaluations across five benchmarks demonstrate that this approach reduces token consumption by over 10 times while maintaining or exceeding the accuracy of strong baselines across various LLMs.

</details>


### [123] [APWA: A Distributed Architecture for Parallelizable Agentic Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15132)
*Evan Rose,Tushin Mallick,Matthew D. Laws,Cristina Nita-Rotaru,Alina Oprea*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型多智能体系统在处理复杂任务时的扩展瓶颈，本文提出了APWA架构，通过将任务解构为无需通信的并行子任务，实现了高效的分布式计算和更强的任务处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统在面对大规模或高度复杂的任务时，往往会遭遇推理效率低、协调困难及计算扩展性不足等瓶颈，难以有效利用并行计算资源来提升吞吐量。

Method: 提出了一种名为“智能体并行工作负载架构”（APWA）的分布式系统。该架构的核心方法是将复杂的工作流自动解构为互不干扰的子问题，使得这些子问题能够在独立的计算资源上并行处理，无需跨节点通信，并支持异构数据处理模式。

Result: 实验表明，APWA能够动态地将复杂查询分解为可并行执行的工作流，并展现出良好的扩展性。在现有系统完全无法处理的大规模任务场景中，APWA依然能够高效完成任务。

Conclusion: APWA架构成功解决了大模型多智能体系统在处理大规模并行任务时的推理与计算瓶颈，通过将工作流解耦为独立的子任务，实现了高效的可扩展性，为复杂任务的分布式处理提供了一种切实可行的范式。

Abstract: Autonomous multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in independently solving complex tasks in a wide breadth of application domains. However, these systems hit critical reasoning, coordination, and computational scaling bottlenecks as the size and complexity of their tasks grow. These limitations hinder multi-agent systems from achieving high-throughput processing for highly parallelizable tasks, despite the availability of parallel computing and reasoning primitives in the underlying LLMs. We introduce the Agent-Parallel Workload Architecture (APWA), a distributed multi-agent system architecture designed for the efficient processing of heavily parallelizable agentic workloads. APWA facilitates parallel execution by decomposing workflows into non-interfering subproblems that can be processed using independent resources without cross-communication. It supports heterogeneous data and parallel processing patterns, and it accommodates tasks from a wide breadth of domains. In our evaluation, we demonstrate that APWA can dynamically decompose complex queries into parallelizable workflows and scales on larger tasks in settings where prior systems fail completely.

</details>


### [124] [OpenDeepThink: Parallel Reasoning via Bradley--Terry Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15177)
*Shang Zhou,Wenhao Chai,Kaiyuan Liu,Huanzhi Mao,Qiuyang Mang,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OpenDeepThink引入了一种基于种群的成对比较（Bradley-Terry）评估机制，取代了不可靠的点对点打分，有效解决了测试时计算中缺乏验证器的问题，显著提升了大模型的推理准确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理扩展主要侧重于增加深度，而通过采样提升广度的方法受限于缺乏客观的真值验证器，且点对点的LLM判分存在噪声和偏见。本研究旨在通过更科学的评估与选择机制来优化测试时计算过程。

Method: 提出OpenDeepThink框架：采用基于种群的优化策略，利用Bradley-Terry模型对多个推理候选进行成对比较，通过投票机制聚合全局排名；在每一代中，对表现优异的候选进行变异（基于自然语言批判），对表现较差的候选进行剔除。此外，构建了高质量的CF-73数据集以验证模型表现。

Result: 在Gemini 3.1 Pro上测试，8轮迭代后Codeforces Elo分提升了405点；在多领域HLE基准测试中，模型在客观可验证领域表现显著提升；该方法具有跨模型泛化能力，无需针对特定模型微调。同时发布了CF-73基准数据集。

Conclusion: OpenDeepThink通过引入基于成对比较的种群进化策略，成功解决了大规模推理任务中缺乏真值验证器（ground-truth verifier）的难题，为提升大语言模型的推理能力提供了一种有效且通用的测试时计算（test-time compute）框架。该方法在客观性较强的任务中表现出色，且具有良好的模型泛化性。

Abstract: Test-time compute scaling is a primary axis for improving LLM reasoning. Existing methods primarily scale depth by extending a single reasoning trace. Scaling breadth by sampling multiple candidates in parallel is straightforward, but introduces a selection bottleneck: choosing the best candidate without a ground-truth verifier, since pointwise LLM judging is noisy and biased. To address this, we introduce OpenDeepThink, a population-based test-time compute framework that selects via pairwise Bradley-Terry comparison. Each generation, the LLM judges random pairs of candidates and aggregates votes via Bradley-Terry into a global ranking; top-ranked candidates are preserved and the top three quarters are mutated using the natural-language critiques produced during comparison; the bottom quarter is discarded. OpenDeepThink raises Gemini 3.1 Pro's effective Codeforces Elo by +405 points in eight sequential LLM-call rounds (~27 minutes wall-clock). The pipeline transfers across weaker and stronger models without retuning, and on the multi-domain HLE benchmark, gains appear concentrated in objectively verifiable domains and reverse in subjective ones. We release CF-73, a curated set of 73 expert-rated Codeforces problems with International Grandmaster annotation and 99% local-evaluation agreement against the official verdict.

</details>

### [125] [Thinking Ahead: Prospection-Guided Retrieval of Memory with Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14177)
*Harshita Chopra,Krishna Kant Chintalapudi,Suman Nath,Ryen W. White,Chirag Shah*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对长程对话中“难以检索语义不相关但历史重要的事实”这一难题，本文提出了一种通过“思维树”预测未来步骤并以此作为检索探针的新型框架（PGR），在多项评估中大幅超越了传统的语义相似度检索方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在长程个性化对话中，现有的基于嵌入（Embedding）相似度或固定图遍历的RAG系统，难以提取出那些与查询词法相似度低但对用户需求至关重要的深层记忆。受人类“前瞻能力”（即利用预想的未来情景作为回忆线索）启发，作者希望通过主动推演来打破“语义相似度”的检索瓶颈。

Method: 本文提出了“前瞻性引导检索”（Prospection-Guided Retrieval, PGR）：1. 不直接基于原始查询进行检索，而是利用思维树（ToT）或链式思维生成多步潜在的“未来步骤”作为检索探针；2. 将检索到的事实反馈回推演过程，实现动态、迭代的记忆发现；3. 构建了MemoryQuest基准测试集，专门评估在低语义相似度约束下的长程记忆检索能力。

Result: 在包含1,625个查询和185个用户配置的基准测试中，PGR-TOT在MemoryQuest上的召回率比最强基线提升了近3倍。在LLM-as-judge和人工盲测评估中，PGR生成的响应在89%-98%的情况下优于现有基线。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于前瞻性（Prospection）的检索框架（PGR），通过将检索过程从被动的语义匹配转向主动的“未来推演”，有效解决了长期对话中记忆提取困难的问题。实验证明，该方法显著提升了模型在复杂、跨会话场景下的记忆召回率和响应质量，为长序列个性化对话系统提供了更有效的记忆管理范式。

Abstract: Long-horizon personalization requires dialogue assistants to retrieve user-specific facts from extended interaction histories. In practice, many relevant facts often have low semanticsimilarity to the query under dense retrieval. Standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and GraphRAG systems are still largely retrospective: they rely on embedding similarity to the query or on fixed graph traversals, so they often miss facts that matter for the user's needs but lie far from the query in embedding space. Inspired by prospection, the human ability to use imagined futures as cues for recall, we introduce Prospection-Guided Retrieval (PGR), which decouples retrieval from how memories are stored. Given a user query, PGR first expands the goal into a short Tree-of-Thought (ToT) or linear chain of plausible next steps, and uses these steps as retrieval probes rather than relying on the original query alone. The facts retrieved by these probes are then used to personalize the next round of prospection, enabling PGR to uncover additional memories that become relevant only after the simulation is grounded in the user's history. We also introduce MemoryQuest, a challenging multi-session benchmark in which each query is annotated with 3--5 dated reference facts subject to a low query-reference similarity constraint. Across 1,625 queries spanning 185 user profiles from 3 publicly available datasets, PGR-TOT substantially improves retrieval, including nearly 3x recall on MemoryQuest over the strongest baseline. In pairwise LLM-as-judge comparisons against baselines, PGR-generated responses are preferred on 89--98% of queries, with blinded human annotations on held-out subsets showing the same trend. Overall, the results demonstrate that explicit prospection yields large gains in long-horizon retrieval and response quality relative to similarity-only baselines.

</details>


### [126] [Efficient Generative Retrieval for E-commerce Search with Semantic Cluster IDs and Expert-Guided RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14434)
*Jianbo Zhu,Xing Fang,Jing Wang,Mingmin Jin,Bokang Wang,Guangxin Song,Zhenyu Xie,Junjie Bai*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种工业级电商搜索生成式召回框架，通过层次化语义标识与专家引导的RL对齐策略，在解决生成式模型实时性与目标一致性问题的同时，显著提升了电商场景下的搜索转化效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式检索虽然具有统一多阶段检索流程的潜力，但在大规模、动态的电商商品库中面临严重的计算延迟问题，且难以直接对齐复杂的下游排序业务目标，导致其在工业级搜索系统中难以落地。

Method: 1. CQ-SID (Category-and-Query constrained Semantic ID)：利用类别感知与查询-商品对比学习，结合残差量化变分自编码器（RQ-VAE）将商品编码为分层语义聚类标识符，从而降低束搜索（Beam Search）的计算复杂度。
2. EG-GRPO (Expert-Guided Group Relative Policy Optimization)：一种基于专家引导的强化学习策略，通过注入真实样本（Ground-truth）来稳定训练过程，有效解决了生成式召回与下游排序目标在稀疏奖励环境下的对齐问题。

Result: 离线实验表明，CQ-SID在语义和个性化点击命中率上较基线提升最高达26.76%和11.11%，同时束搜索规模减半；在线A/B测试显示GMV提升1.15%，UCTCVR提升0.40%；在生产环境中，该生成式召回通道已承担了超过50%的曝光和近73%的购买贡献。

Conclusion: 本文验证了将生成式检索作为召回阶段的补充方案在工业级电商场景中的有效性。通过层次化语义ID设计与专家引导的强化学习对齐策略，成功解决了生成式模型在超大规模动态商品库下的延迟与业务对齐难题，为生成式检索在实际生产环境中的落地提供了成熟的范式。

Abstract: Generative retrieval offers a promising alternative by unifying the fragmented multi-stage retrieval process into a single end-to-end model. However, its practical adoption in industrial e-commerce search remains challenging, given the massive and dynamic product catalogs, strict latency requirements, and the need to align retrieval with downstream ranking goals. In this work, we propose a retrieval framework tailored for real-world recall scenarios, positioning generative retrieval as a recall-stage supplement rather than an end-to-end replacement. Our method, CQ-SID (Category-and-Query constrained Semantic ID), employs category-aware and query-item contrastive learning along with Residual Quantized VAEs to encode items into hierarchical semantic cluster identifiers, significantly reducing beam search complexity. Additionally, we develop EG-GRPO (Expert-Guided Group Relative Policy Optimization), a reinforcement learning approach that aligns generative recall with downstream ranking under sparse rewards by injecting ground-truth samples to stabilize training. Offline experiments on TmallAPP search logs show that CQ-SID achieves up to 26.76% and 11.11% relative gains in semantic and personalized click hitrate over RQ-VAE baselines, while halving beam search size. EG-GRPO further improves multi-objective performance. Online A/B tests confirm gains in GMV (+1.15%) and UCTCVR (+0.40%). The generative recall channel now contributes substantially in production, accounting for over 50.25% of exposures, 58.96% of clicks, and 72.63% of purchases, demonstrating a viable path for deploying generative retrieval in real-world e-commerce systems.

### [127] [Stop Overthinking: Unlocking Efficient Listwise Reranking with Minimal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14450)
*Danyang Liu,Kan Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对大模型重排序中“过度思考”导致的推理成本高昂问题，本文提出了一种基于帕累托筛选的自蒸馏框架，通过学习高效的精简推理路径，在不牺牲性能的前提下大幅降低了计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于思维链（CoT）的推理增强重排序模型虽然性能卓越，但往往需要生成大量冗余的推理Token，导致计算成本过高，无法满足延迟敏感应用的需求。研究旨在解决这种性能提升与计算成本之间的矛盾。

Method: 提出了一种长度正则化的自蒸馏框架：首先从教师模型（Rank-K）采样多样化的推理路径；其次应用帕累托最优筛选策略，选取在保持高性能的同时消耗Token最少的推理轨迹；最后利用这些精简的高质量推理路径对学生模型进行微调，使其学习并内化高效的推理模式，从而消除冗余的思考过程。

Result: 在TREC Deep Learning和NeuCLIR基准测试中，该方法能够在保持与教师模型相当的检索效果的同时，将推理阶段的Token消耗减少了34%至37%。

Conclusion: 研究证实了“过度思考”现象的存在，即过长的推理过程并不必然带来性能提升。提出的Length-Regularized Self-Distillation框架通过蒸馏精简且高效的推理路径，有效平衡了检索性能与计算成本，为推理增强型重排序模型在延迟敏感场景下的部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Listwise reranking utilizing Large Language Models (LLMs) has achieved state-of-the-art retrieval effectiveness. Recently, reasoning-enhanced models have further pushed these boundaries by employing Chain-of-Thought (CoT) to perform deep comparative analysis of candidate documents. However, this performance gain comes at a prohibitive computational cost, as models often generate thousands of reasoning tokens before producing a final ranking. In this work, we investigate the relationship between reasoning length and ranking quality, revealing an overthinking phenomenon where extended reasoning yields diminishing returns. To address this, we propose a Length-Regularized Self-Distillation framework. We synthesize a dataset by sampling diverse reasoning traces from a teacher model (Rank-K) and applying a Pareto-inspired filter to select traces that achieve high ranking performance with minimal token usage. By fine-tuning on these concise, high-quality rationales, the student model learns to internalize efficient reasoning patterns, effectively pruning redundant deliberation. Experiments on TREC Deep Learning and NeuCLIR benchmarks demonstrate that our method maintains the teacher's effectiveness while reducing inference token consumption by 34%-37% across different retrieval settings, offering a practical solution for deploying reasoning-enhanced rerankers in latency-sensitive applications.

</details>


### [128] [Asymmetric Generative Recommendation via Multi-Expert Projection and Multi-Faceted Hierarchical Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14512)
*Bin Huang,Xin Wang,Junwei Pan,Yongqi Zhou,Yifeng Zhou,Zhixiang Feng,Shudong Huang,Haijie Gu,Wenwu Zhu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对生成式推荐模型在处理离散 ID 时存在的输入和输出信息瓶颈问题，AsymRec 提出了一种非对称架构，通过连续输入投影和分层离散化输出，显著提升了模型在长尾物品推荐和语义捕捉上的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成式推荐（GenRec）模型通常将推荐任务视为序列生成，并使用相同的离散语义 ID 作为输入和输出（即对称设计）。作者指出这种设计存在两个关键的信息瓶颈：一是“输入瓶颈”，即量化会导致语义丢失且模型易受流行度偏差影响；二是“输出瓶颈”，即离散目标的精度不足，限制了监督信号的质量。

Method: 作者提出了 AsymRec 框架，核心在于解耦输入和输出表示：1) 多专家语义投影（MSP）：利用专家混合（MoE）思想，将连续特征映射到 Transformer 隐空间，保留了丰富的语义信息并增强了对长尾物品的泛化能力；2) 多面分层量化（MHQ）：通过多视角和多层级量化构建高容量、结构化的离散目标，并引入语义正则化以防止维度坍塌，提升了预测目标的精确度。

Result: 在广泛的实验评估中，AsymRec 在多个数据集上表现优异，平均比当前最先进的生成式推荐模型提升了 15.8%，验证了其在缓解信息瓶颈和提升推荐质量方面的有效性。

Conclusion: AsymRec 通过打破生成式推荐在输入和输出端对离散 ID 的对称依赖，有效缓解了信息瓶颈问题。该框架不仅验证了非对称设计在提升推荐性能上的优势，也为未来生成式推荐模型的设计提供了新的范式，特别是在处理长尾物品和细粒度语义方面具有显著价值。

Abstract: Generative Recommendation (GenRec) models reformulate recommendation as a sequence generation task, representing items as discrete Semantic IDs used symmetrically as both inputs and prediction targets. We identify a critical dual-stage information bottleneck in this design: (1) the Input Bottleneck, where lossy quantization degrades fine-grained semantics, while popularity bias skews the learned representations toward frequent items, and (2) the Output Bottleneck, where imprecise discrete targets limit supervision quality. To address these issues, we propose AsymRec, an asymmetric continuous-discrete framework that decouples input and output representations. Specifically, Multi-expert Semantic Projection (MSP) maps continuous embeddings into the Transformer's hidden space via expert-specialized projections, preserving semantic richness and improving generalization to infrequent items. Multi-faceted Hierarchical Quantization (MHQ) constructs high-capacity, structured discrete targets through multi-view and multi-level quantization with semantic regularization, preventing dimensional collapse while retaining fine-grained distinctions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AsymRec consistently outperforms state-of-the-art generative recommenders by an average of 15.8 %. The code will be released.

</details>


### [129] [Discrimination Is Generation: Unifying Ranking and Retrieval from a Tokenizer Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14853)
*Shuli Wang,Junwei Yin,Changhao Li,Senjie Kou,Chi Wang,Yinqiu Huang,Yinhua Zhu,Haitao Wang,Xingxing Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 DIG 框架，通过将分词器嵌入排序模型进行端到端训练，打破了生成式检索与判别式排序之间的壁垒，实现了更强的个性化推荐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成式推荐系统中的语义ID（SIDs）训练与排序任务脱节，导致生成式检索在个性化表现上持续落后于判别式排序模型。核心动机在于解决“排序是在物品空间取 argmax，而检索是在 Token 空间取 argmax”这一本质上一致但粒度不同的问题，从而实现生成与判别的统一。

Method: 提出名为 DIG（Discrimination Is Generation）的框架，将分词器（Tokenizer）嵌入到判别式排序模型中进行端到端联合训练。该方法利用特征分配分类法（Feature Assignment Taxonomy），将物品固有特征编码为 SIDs，并通过用户-物品交叉特征（u2i）引导码本边界，同时引入 MLP_u2t 蒸馏模块，在推理阶段将 u2i 近似应用于 Token 层级。

Result: 在三个公开基准测试和两个工业数据集上的实验表明，DIG 框架能同时提升检索质量、排序质量以及统一检索-排序的效果，证明了端到端范式的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将检索器（Tokenizer）嵌入判别式排序模型中，成功弥合了生成式推荐与判别式排序之间的鸿沟，证明了通过端到端训练构建语义ID（SIDs）能显著提升生成式检索的个性化能力，并实现了检索与排序任务的协同优化。

Abstract: Semantic IDs (SIDs) define the generation space of generative recommendation and directly determine its personalization ceiling. However, existing tokenizers are trained independently with retrieval objectives, leaving personalization signals fully decoupled from the SID construction process -- a fundamental gap that causes generative retrieval to persistently lag behind discriminative ranking. In this paper, we rethink the essence of SIDs: \emph{ranking seeks argmax in item space while retrieval seeks argmax in token space; both are the same problem solved at different granularities.} Based on this insight, we propose \DIG (\textbf{D}iscrimination \textbf{I}s \textbf{G}eneration), which embeds the tokenizer inside a discriminative ranking model for end-to-end training -- the ranker naturally becomes a retrieval model, yielding two models from a single training run. \DIG is organized around a \emph{feature assignment taxonomy}: item-intrinsic static features are encoded into SIDs, user-item cross features (u2i) implicitly drive codebook boundaries toward recommendation decision boundaries during training, and an MLP$_\mathrm{u2t}$ distillation module approximates u2i at the token level for inference. Experiments on three public benchmarks and two industrial datasets demonstrate that \DIG simultaneously improves ranking, retrieval, and unified retrieval-ranking quality.

</details>

### [130] [Vision-Based Runtime Monitoring under Varying Specifications using Semantic Latent Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13923)
*Bardh Hoxha,Oliver Schön,Hideki Okamoto,Lars Lindemann,Georgios Fainekos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可重用的视觉运行时监控框架，通过预测时序原子的鲁棒性基准，利用一致性预测为任意时序逻辑公式提供严格的有限样本认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在视觉驱动的自主系统中，如何在部分可观测环境下，高效、可重用且具备有限样本保证地对过去时序逻辑（ptSTL）进行运行时监控。

Method: 1. 提出语义基础方法：通过预测时序原子的鲁棒性得分向量作为最小预测目标，并利用单次一致性校准实现整个公式片段的认证。2. 提出滚动预测监控：仅预测当前谓词值并在线重构历史。3. 利用单调的1-Lipschitz可重用接口，通过确定性解码器对公式进行评估，无需联合界（union bound）。

Result: 在行人十字路口基准测试和Waymo数据集上的实验表明：语义基础方法在长时域下精度提升显著（达4倍），而滚动预测监控在短时域下更紧凑；两种方法均在经验上满足了一致性覆盖保证。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于语义基础和一致性预测的鲁棒监控框架，能够在部分可观测的视觉环境中，为任意时序逻辑公式提供有效的有限样本认证，解决了模型重用性和认证效率的问题。

Abstract: We study certified runtime monitoring of past-time signal temporal logic (ptSTL) from visual observations under partial observability. The monitor must infer safety-relevant quantities from images and provide finite-sample guarantees, while being \emph{reusable}: once trained and calibrated, it should certify any formula in a target fragment without per-formula retraining. For fragments induced by a finite dictionary of temporal atoms, we prove that the \emph{semantic basis}, the vector of atom robustness scores, is the minimum prediction target within the class of monotone, 1-Lipschitz reusable interfaces: any formula is evaluated by a deterministic decoder derived from the parse tree, and a single conformal calibration pass certifies the entire fragment with no union bound. We also introduce a \emph{rolling prediction monitor} that predicts only current predicate values and reconstructs temporal history online; this is easier to learn but grows conservative at long horizons. On a pedestrian-crossroad benchmark, rolling achieves tighter certified bounds at short horizons while the semantic-basis monitor is up to 4-times tighter at long horizons. We validate the presented monitors on real-world Waymo driving data, where both monitors satisfy the conformal coverage guarantee empirically.

</details>


### [131] [Mechanistic Interpretability of EEG Foundation Models via Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13930)
*William Lehn-Schiøler,Magnus Ruud Kjær,Rahul Thapa,Magnus Guldberg Pedersen,Anton Storgaard Mosquera,Nick Williams,Radu Gatej,Tue Lehn-Schiøler,Sándor Beniczky,Sadasivan Puthusserypady,James Zou,Lars Kai Hansen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）破解了EEG基础模型的黑盒机制，通过概念操纵与光谱解码技术，不仅实现了对临床病理特征的透明化解释，还验证了对模型内部表征进行精准医疗干预的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG基础模型虽然在临床任务中表现出色，但其决策机制呈现“黑盒”状态，缺乏可解释性，这成为了临床应用和建立信任的主要障碍。研究旨在通过解析模型内部的稀疏表征，实现对模型决策过程的解耦与透明化。

Method: 研究应用TopK稀疏自编码器（SAEs）对三种不同的EEG Transformer架构（SleepFM、REVE、LaBraM）进行特征提取，通过构建临床分类体系进行单语义性基准测试，并引入“目标与非目标”探针度量指标进行概念操纵（concept steering）和光谱解码。

Result: 研究证明了稀疏特征可以在不同架构间稳健迁移；识别出了模型的三种操作状态（可选择性操纵、编码但纠缠、未编码）；揭示了年龄与病理特征纠缠等表征缺陷，并成功通过光谱解码将潜在空间的操作转化为可解释的生理频率特征。

Conclusion: 本研究通过稀疏自编码器成功揭示了EEG基础模型内部的表征机制，不仅提升了模型的可解释性，还通过概念操纵技术实现了对病理特征的精准干预，为临床应用提供了更透明、可控的技术路径。

Abstract: EEG foundation models achieve state-of-the-art clinical performance, yet the internal computations driving their predictions remain opaque: a barrier to clinical trust. We apply TopK Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) across three architecturally distinct EEG transformers: SleepFM, REVE, and LaBraM to extract sparse feature dictionaries from their embeddings. By grounding these features in a clinical taxonomy (abnormality, age, sex, and medication), we benchmark monosemanticity and entanglement across architectures. A single hyperparameter procedure, driven by an intrinsic dictionary health audit, transfers robustly across all three architectures. Via concept steering, we introduce a "target vs. off-target" probe area metric to quantify steering selectivity and reveal three operational regimes: selectively steerable, encoded but entangled, and non-encoded. This framework exposes critical representational failures: "wrecking-ball" interventions that collapse global model performance, and clinical entanglements, such as age-pathology confounding, where it is impossible to suppress one concept without corrupting the other. Finally, a spectral decoder maps these interventions back to the amplitude spectrum, translating latent manipulations into physiologically interpretable frequency signatures, such as pathological slow-wave suppression and $α$-band restoration.

</details>


### [132] [Rethinking Molecular OOD Generalization via Target-Aware Source Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13932)
*Zhuohao Lin,Kun Li,Jiameng Chen,Jiajun Yu,Duanhua Cao,Yizhen Zheng,Wenbin Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对分子性质预测在极端分布外（OOD）场景下的性能瓶颈，本文提出了SCOPE-BENCH评估基准和POMA自适应框架，通过智能数据检索与双尺度领域对齐，显著提升了模型在复杂分子结构上的预测泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分子性质预测模型在极端OOD场景下表现不佳，主要因为：1. 传统的支架分割（scaffold-splitting）无法避免微观语义重叠，导致模型产生捷径学习；2. 传统的领域自适应方法在处理极端结构差异时，容易引入拓扑噪声并触发负迁移。

Method: 1. 提出了SCOPE-BENCH：一种基于物理化学描述符空间进行簇级划分的OOD性能评估基准。
2. 提出了POMA框架：采用“检索-组合-自适应”流程，利用强化学习策略从多源数据中自适应选择最优子集，并进行宏观拓扑与微观药效团尺度的双尺度领域自适应。

Result: 1. 在SCOPE-BENCH上，现有先进3D分子模型的预测误差大幅上升（最高达8.0倍，平均5.9倍）。
2. POMA框架在不同骨干架构下表现优异，平均绝对误差（MAE）最高降低了11.2%，平均相对提升达6.2%。

Conclusion: 通过构建更具挑战性的SCOPE-BENCH基准，研究揭示了现有分子性质预测模型在极端分布外（OOD）场景下的脆弱性。POMA框架通过智能的知识检索、策略优化和双尺度领域自适应，有效缓解了负迁移问题，为AI辅助药物发现中的鲁棒性预测提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Robust prediction of molecular properties under extreme out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios is a pivotal bottleneck in AI-driven drug discovery. Current scaffold-splitting protocols fail to obstruct microscopic semantic overlap, predisposing models to shortcut learning and overestimating their true extrapolation capability; meanwhile, conventional domain adaptation paradigms suffer under extreme structural shifts, as blindly aligning heterogeneous source libraries injects topological noise and triggers negative transfer. To address these two challenges, scaffold-cluster out-of-distribution performance evaluation benchmark (SCOPE-BENCH), a benchmark built on cluster-level partitioning in an explicit physicochemical descriptor space, is proposed alongside policy optimization for multi-source adaptation (POMA), a framework that formulates knowledge transfer as a retrieve-compose-adapt pipeline: labeled source scaffolds structurally close to the unlabeled target are first identified as proxy targets; a reinforcement learning policy then adaptively selects the optimal source subset from an exponentially large candidate pool; and dual-scale domain adaptation is finally performed at macroscopic topological and microscopic pharmacophore scales. Evaluations show that prediction errors of state-of-the-art 3D molecular models surge by up to 8.0x on SCOPE-BENCH with a mean of 5.9x, while POMA achieves up to an 11.2% reduction in mean absolute error with an average relative improvement of 6.2% across diverse backbone architectures. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Molecular-OOD-Code-73F6.

</details>


### [133] [Unsupervised learning of acquisition variability in structural connectomes via hybrid latent space modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13933)
*Gaurav Rudravaram,Lianrui Zuo,Karthik Ramadass,Elyssa McMaster,Jongyeon Yoon,Aravind R. Krishnan,Adam M. Saunders,Chenyu Gao,Nancy R. Newlin,Praitayini Kanakaraj,Lori L. Beason Held,Murat Bilgel,Laura A. Barquero,Micah DArchangel,Tin Q. Nguyen,Laurie B. Cutting,Derek Archer,Timothy J. Hohman,Daniel C. Moyer,Bennett A. Landman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对dMRI数据采集差异导致的分析误差，本研究提出了一种创新的无监督深度学习框架，通过“架构退火”自动分离采集参数效应与生物变异，显著提升了结构连接组分析的准确性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于不同站点、扫描仪和成像协议导致的采集差异，弥散磁共振成像（dMRI）数据的结构连接组分析面临巨大挑战。传统降维方法难以区分采集差异与真实的生物学变异，而现有的混合潜在空间模型又过于依赖人工手动调节，因此需要一种自动化的解耦方法。

Method: 引入了一种基于架构退火（Architectural Annealing）的无监督深度学习框架。该模型在编码器输出端动态调整，实现了离散变量（表征采集相关效应）与连续变量（表征生物学变异）之间的自适应平衡，无需手动调整容量，克服了传统混合潜在空间模型依赖超参数调优的局限性。

Result: 在包含7,416个结构连接组的大规模数据集上，该模型表现出色。在采集站点识别任务中达到了最高的调整兰德指数（ARI=0.53），证明了其在无监督环境下有效分离扫描参数效应的能力，且在处理老年痴呆症（AD）及轻度认知障碍（MCI）相关数据时表现稳健。

Conclusion: 通过架构退火而非传统的损失函数退火，研究提出了一种有效的无监督框架。该方法能更好地将dMRI数据中的采集变异（扫描仪、协议）与生物学变异（年龄、疾病状态）解耦，在连接组分析中展现出更优的潜在空间表征能力。

Abstract: Acquisition differences across sites, scanners, and protocols in dMRI introduce variability that complicates structural connectome analysis. This motivates deep learning models that can represent high-dimensional connectomes in a low-dimensional space while explicitly separating acquisition-related effects from biological variation. Conventional dimensionality reduction methods model all variance as continuous, so acquisition effects often get absorbed into a continuous latent space. Recent hybrid latent-space models combine discrete and continuous components to address this, but typically require manual capacity tuning to ensure the discrete component captures the intended variability. We introduce an unsupervised framework that removes this manual tuning by architecturally annealing encoder outputs before decoding, allowing the model to adaptively balance discrete and continuous latent variables during training. To evaluate it, we curated a dataset of N=7,416 structural connectomes derived from dMRI, spanning ages 2 to 102 and 13 studies with 25 unique acquisition-parameter combinations. Of these, 5,900 are cognitively unimpaired, 877 have mild cognitive impairment (MCI), and 639 have Alzheimer's disease (AD). We compare against a standard VAE, PCA with k-means clustering, and hybrid models that anneal only through the loss function. Our architectural annealing produces stronger site learning (ARI=0.53, p<0.05) than these baselines. Results show that a hybrid continuous-discrete latent space, with architectural rather than loss-based annealing, provides a useful unsupervised mechanism for capturing acquisition variability in dMRI: by jointly modeling smooth and categorical structure, the Joint-VAE recovers clusters aligned with scanner and protocol differences.

</details>


### [134] [Towards the Next Frontier of LLMs, Training on Private Data: A Cross-Domain Benchmark for Federated Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13936)
*Daniel M. Jimenez-Gutierrez,Enrique Zuazua,Georgios Kellaris,Joaquin del Rio,Oleksii Sliusarenko,Xabi Uribe-Etxebarria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于联邦学习的大语言模型参数高效微调框架，成功解决了医疗和金融等受监管领域数据隐私保护与跨机构协作的矛盾，在保持数据本地化的前提下，实现了大模型在非独立同分布数据上的高效适配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的进一步发展受限于公共数据的枯竭，而价值极高的私有领域数据（如医疗和金融）因隐私、监管及组织壁垒无法共享。此外，这些数据通常具有非独立同分布（non-IID）特征，直接集中训练存在困难，因此需要一种无需共享原始数据即可利用这些私有数据的方法。

Method: 研究人员基于 Sherpa.ai 联邦学习平台，采用联邦微调框架，在不交换原始隐私数据的前提下，联合多方共同对大模型进行参数高效微调（PEFT）。评估了 LoRA、QLoRA 和 IA3 三种 PEFT 策略在 MedQA、MedMCQA、FPB 和 FiQA-SA 四个跨领域数据集上的表现，并模拟了真实环境下的非独立同分布（non-IID）数据异构性。

Result: 实验表明，联邦微调的效果接近集中式训练，且显著优于单个机构孤立学习的效果。从绿色人工智能（Green AI）的角度来看，QLoRA 和 IA3 能够以极小的精度损失显著提升效率。

Conclusion: 联邦参数高效微调（Federated PEFT）是一种在保护数据隐私的同时，有效利用分散在各机构中的私有数据来提升大语言模型（LLM）领域性能的可行且高效的方案。

Abstract: The recent success of large language models (LLMs) has been largely driven by vast public datasets. However, the next frontier for LLM development lies beyond public data. Much of the world's most valuable information is private, especially in highly regulated sectors such as healthcare and finance, where data include patient histories or customer communications. Unlocking this data could represent a major leap forward, enabling LLMs with deeper domain expertise and stronger real-world utility. Yet, these data cannot be shared because they are distributed across institutions and constrained by privacy, regulatory, and organizational barriers. Moreover, institutional datasets are typically non-independent and identically distributed (non-IID), differing across sites in population characteristics, data modalities, documentation patterns, and task-specific label distributions.
  In this paper, we demonstrate a practical approach to unlocking private and distributed institutional data for LLM adaptation through federated collaboration across data silos. Built on the Sherpa.ai Federated Learning platform, our framework enables nodes to jointly fine-tune a shared LLM without exchanging private data. We evaluate this approach through a cross-domain benchmark in healthcare and finance, using four closed-ended question answering and classification datasets: MedQA, MedMCQA, FPB, and FiQA-SA. We compare three parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) strategies-LoRA, QLoRA, and IA3-across pretrained backbones under non-IID settings reflecting institutional data heterogeneity. Our results show that federated fine-tuning performs close to centralized training and outperforms isolated single-institution learning. From a Green AI perspective, QLoRA and IA3 improve efficiency with limited accuracy degradation, supporting federated PEFT as a viable approach for adapting LLMs where data cannot be shared.

</details>


### [135] [A Unified Geometric Framework for Weighted Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13943)
*Raphael Vock,Edouard Duchesnay,Benoit Dufumier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过距离几何视角分析了对比学习的加权目标函数，发现权重设计直接决定了嵌入空间的几何质量。研究揭示了现有算法在面对数据不平衡或特定标签结构时的失败机制，并为设计几何一致性强的对比学习目标提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对比学习在表征空间几何结构方面的理解尚显不足，特别是对于不同权重方案如何影响最终嵌入分布缺乏系统性理论框架，导致在处理类别不平衡或连续标签时易出现性能瓶颈或退化现象。

Method: 将加权InfoNCE目标函数转化为“距离几何问题”（Distance Geometry Problem），通过解析权重方案与嵌入目标几何之间的映射关系，对监督和弱监督学习场景下的最优嵌入进行数学表征和几何分析。

Result: 研究发现：1. 在监督学习中，SupCon在类别不平衡时会产生非均匀的类间相似度，而Soft SupCon能保持正则单纯形（Regular Simplex）几何结构；2. 在连续标签设置中，y-Aware CL因欧几里得标签权重与球体潜在相似度之间的失配而难以达到最优；3. 提出了几何一致性设计准则（如Euclidean-Euclidean weighting），以确保对比学习目标的有效实现。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了对比学习中权重方案（Weighting Scheme）对嵌入空间几何结构的决定性影响。研究表明，通过将加权InfoNCE目标函数解释为距离几何问题，可以设计出更加稳健的对比学习目标，避免因几何不一致导致的表示退化或性能失效。

Abstract: Contrastive learning (CL) aims to preserve relational structure between samples by learning representations that reflect a similarity graph. Yet, the geometry of the resulting embeddings remains poorly understood. Here we show that weighted InfoNCE objectives can be interpreted as Distance Geometry Problems, where the weighting scheme specifies the target geometry to be realized by the representation. This viewpoint yields exact characterizations of the optimal embeddings for several supervised and weakly supervised objectives. In supervised classification, both SupCon and Soft SupCon (a dense relaxation of it where pairs from distinct classes have small non-zero similarity) collapse samples within each class to a single prototype. However, while balanced SupCon recovers the classical regular simplex geometry, class imbalance breaks this symmetry: SupCon induces non-uniform inter-class similarities depending on class sizes, whereas Soft SupCon preserves a regular simplex geometry regardless of class imbalance. In continuous-label settings, our framework reveals a different failure mode: y-Aware CL generally cannot attain its entropic optimum unless the labels lie on a hypersphere, exposing a mismatch between Euclidean label weights and spherical latent similarity. By contrast, geometrically consistent choices such as Euclidean-Euclidean weighting or X-CLR admit unique optimal embeddings. Our results show that the choice of weighting scheme determines whether contrastive learning is geometrically realizable, degenerate, or inconsistent, providing a principled framework for designing contrastive objectives.

*Sinjae Kang,Chanyoung Kim,Kaixin Wang,Li Zhao,Kimin Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文引入了WarmPrior，一种利用近期动作历史来改进机器人控制生成式模型源分布的方法。通过拉直生成路径，该技术显著提升了机器人操作任务的成功率、样本效率及整体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于扩散和流匹配的机器人控制策略大多采用标准高斯分布作为源分布。然而，这种静态先验未能充分利用机器人的动作历史信息，导致生成路径复杂，且在强化学习探索中缺乏效率。作者旨在通过改进源分布来优化生成过程。

Method: 提出了一种名为WarmPrior的方法，用基于近期动作历史的、具有时间基础的先验分布，取代了生成式模型（如扩散模型和流匹配模型）中标准的静态高斯源分布。该方法通过引导生成模型从更接近真实动作轨迹的初始点开始采样，从而简化了生成路径。

Result: 在机器人操作任务中，使用WarmPrior能够显著拉直生成过程中的概率路径，从而提升模仿学习的成功率；在先验空间强化学习中，该方法也提高了样本效率和最终的执行性能。

Conclusion: 论文指出，源分布的设计是生成式机器人控制中一个关键且被低估的维度。通过引入WarmPrior，不仅可以优化生成过程的动力学路径，还能有效提升模仿学习和强化学习在机器人操作任务中的性能。

Abstract: Generative policies based on diffusion and flow matching have become a dominant paradigm for visuomotor robotic control. We show that replacing the standard Gaussian source distribution with WarmPrior, a simple temporally grounded prior constructed from readily available recent action history, consistently improves success rates on robotic manipulation tasks. We trace this gain to markedly straighter probability paths, echoing the effect of optimal-transport couplings in Rectified Flow. Beyond standard behavior cloning, WarmPrior also reshapes the exploration distribution in prior-space reinforcement learning, improving both sample efficiency and final performance. Collectively, these results identify the source distribution as an important and underexplored design axis in generative robot control.

### [137] [Towards Resource-Efficient LLMs: End-to-End Energy Accounting of Distillation Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13981)
*Katherine Lambert,Sasha Luccioni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过建立全面的能源核算框架，揭示了蒸馏流程中常被忽视的教师模型端能耗，并为在有限能源预算下优化模型蒸馏提供了量化分析方法与实操准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究指出，蒸馏过程的能源成本被严重低估。通过构建全面且透明的能源核算框架，研究者揭示了教师模型端（如数据生成和Logit缓存）的隐藏能耗，并为在能源约束下进行高效的模型蒸馏提供了关键的设计指导原则。

Abstract: The rise in deployment of large language models has driven a surge in GPU demand and datacenter scaling, raising concerns about electricity use, grid stress, and the impacts of modern AI workloads. Distillation is often promoted as one of the most effective paths to obtain cheaper, more efficient models, yet these claims rarely account for the full end-to-end energy and resource costs, including crucial teacher-side workloads such as data generation, logit caching, and evaluation. We present a comprehensive energy accounting framework that measures the complete computational cost of distillation pipelines via detailed stage-wise tracking of GPU device power consumption. In our experiments, we separate and log empirical energy use across distinct phases and systematically measure the energy and emissions of two common distillation methods: the classic logit-based knowledge distillation and synthetic-data supervised fine-tuning, constructing energy-quality Pareto frontiers that expose the previously ignored costs. From these measurements and analyses, we derive practical design rules for selecting distillation methods and hyperparameters under energy and budget constraints, and release an open-source measurement harness and accounting protocol to provide a standardized foundation for comparable, reproducible distillation research, explicitly accountable for complete pipeline energy impact.

### [138] [TabPFN-3: Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13986)
*Léo Grinsztajn,Klemens Flöge,Oscar Key,Felix Birkel,Philipp Jund,Brendan Roof,Mihir Manium,Shi Bin,Hoo,Magnus Bühler,Anurag Garg,Dominik Safaric,Jake Robertson,Benjamin Jäger,Simone Alessi,Adrian Hayler,Vladyslav Moroshan,Lennart Purucker,Philipp Singer,Alan Arazi,Julien Siems,Jan Hendrik Metzen,Georg Grab,Nick Erickson,Siyuan Guo,Eliott Kalfon,Simon Bing,David Salinas,Clara Cornu,Lilly Charlotte Wehrhahn,Diana Kriuchkova,Kursat Kaya,Lydia Sidhoum,Marie Salmon,Jerry Chen,Madelon Hulsebos,Yann LeCun,Samuel Müller,Bernhard Schölkopf,Sauraj Gambhir,Noah Hollmann,Frank Hutter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TabPFN-3 是一款通过纯合成数据预训练的下一代表格基础模型，实现了对百万行规模数据的支持，速度提升 20 倍，并通过测试时计算扩展（Thinking 模式）在多项基准测试中刷新了 SOTA，是当前表格机器学习领域极具竞争力的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管 TabPFN 在表格数据领域已展现出潜力，但在处理大规模数据集（百万行级）、复杂数据类型（时序、关系型、文本）以及推理速度和计算效率方面仍存在局限性，需要构建一个更可扩展、更快且泛化能力更强的新一代表格基础模型。

Method: 1. 基于 Prior-data 预训练：完全依赖合成数据进行预训练，无需真实数据或大语言模型。
2. 架构优化：引入行分块（row-chunking）技术和优化的 KV 缓存，支持处理高达 100 万行的训练数据。
3. 测试时计算扩展：通过 TabPFN-3-Plus (Thinking) 模式，在推理阶段利用增加的计算资源来提升预测精度。
4. 针对性扩展：开发了专门的检查点（如 TabPFN-TS-3），以适配时序、关系型数据及表格-文本数据。

Result: 1. 性能领先：在 TabArena 基准测试中大幅超越各类基准模型（包括调优后的梯度提升树），在 Thinking 模式下 Elo 分数提升 200 以上。
2. 效率提升：相比前代模型速度提升达 20 倍；SHAP 值计算速度提升 120 倍。
3. 规模化：在单张 H100 GPU 上即可支持 100 万行数据的处理。
4. 领域广泛：在 RelBenchV1 和 TabSTAR 等多个领域基准测试中达到行业领先水平（SOTA）。

Conclusion: TabPFN-3 标志着表格数据基础模型的重大飞跃，通过引入测试时计算扩展（test-time compute scaling）和优化的架构，在处理大规模数据集时实现了性能与效率的双重突破，证明了纯合成数据预训练模型在各种复杂表格场景中的通用性和先进性。

Abstract: Tabular data underpins most high-value prediction problems in science and industry, and TabPFN has driven the foundation model revolution for this modality. Designed with feedback from our users, TabPFN-3 builds on this foundation to scale state-of-the-art performance to datasets with 1M training rows and substantially reduce training and inference time. Pretrained exclusively on synthetic data from our prior, TabPFN-3 dramatically pushes the frontier of tabular prediction and brings substantial gains on time series, relational, and tabular-text data. On the standard tabular benchmark TabArena, a forward pass of TabPFN-3 outperforms all other models, including tuned and ensembled baselines, by a significant margin, and pareto-dominates the speed/performance frontier. On more diverse datasets, TabPFN-3 ranks first on datasets with many classes, and beats 8-hour-tuned gradient-boosted-tree baselines on datasets up to 1M training rows and 200 features. TabPFN-3 introduces test-time compute scaling to tabular foundation models. Our API offering TabPFN-3-Plus (Thinking) exploits this to beat all non-TabPFN models by over 200 Elo on TabArena, rising to 420 Elo on the largest data subset, and outperforms AutoGluon 1.5 extreme while being 10x faster, without using LLMs, real data, internet search or any other model besides TabPFN. TabPFN-3 extends the capabilities of our models, enabling SOTA prediction on relational data (new SOTA foundation model on RelBenchV1) and tabular-text data (SOTA on TabSTAR via TabPFN-3-Plus); and improves existing integrations: a specialized checkpoint, TabPFN-TS-3, ranks 2nd on the time-series benchmark fev-bench, and SHAP-value computation is up to 120x faster. TabPFN-3 achieves this performance while being up to 20x faster than TabPFN-2.5. In addition, a reduced KV cache and row-chunking scale to 1M rows on one H100 with fast inference speed.

### [139] [Support Before Frequency in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13999)
*Adrian Müller,Antoine Gonon,Zebang Shen,Ya-Ping Hsieh,Niao He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了离散扩散模型在语言建模中的学习机制，证明了模型遵循“先学习数据结构/有效性，后学习频率分布”的演进规律，并分析了不同扩散机制对这一过程的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管离散扩散模型在语言建模中表现出色，但目前尚不清楚其去噪目标是如何组织学习过程的，特别是模型学习数据分布中不同特征（如结构有效性与词频分布）的先后顺序。

Method: 研究者在小噪声体制下，通过数学推导分析了离散扩散模型中单标记逆向编辑的过程。他们将逆向过程分解为决定数据支持（有效性）的“主导尺度”和决定相对频率的“系数”两部分。此外，通过掩码语言扩散模型和合成正则语言任务进行了实证验证。

Result: 研究发现：1. 离散扩散模型确实存在学习阶段分离现象；2. 恢复有效性结构仅需学习逆向概率的量级，而恢复数据频率则需要更精确的系数估计；3. 吸收扩散（Masking）机制在学习有效性方面比均匀扩散更具针对性；4. 实验证实“支持定位”的学习早于“支持内频率排序”的学习。

Conclusion: 离散扩散模型在学习过程中表现出明显的阶段性：模型倾向于优先学习数据的支持集（即语法有效性结构），然后再精细化调整数据分布的频率信息。这一过程与扩散机制的类型（如均匀扩散或吸收扩散）密切相关。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are increasingly competitive for language modeling, yet it remains unclear how their denoising objectives organize learning. Although these objectives target the full data distribution, we show that the exact reverse process induces a hierarchy between coarse support information and finer frequency information. For uniform and absorbing (a.k.a. masking) diffusion, we prove that, in the small-noise regime of the final denoising steps, each single-token reverse edit decomposes into a leading scale, determined by whether it moves toward the data support (e.g., grammatically valid sentences), and a finer coefficient, determining relative probabilities within the same scale. Thus, recovering validity structure only requires learning the correct order of magnitude of reverse probabilities, whereas recovering data frequencies requires coefficient-level estimation. The separation is mechanism-dependent: uniform diffusion exhibits a trichotomy into validity-improving, validity-preserving, and validity-worsening edits, while absorbing diffusion places its leading-order mass on validity-improving moves. Experiments on a masked language diffusion model and synthetic regular-language tasks support these predictions: support-localization emerges earlier than within-support frequency ranking, and the contrast between uniform and absorbing diffusion matches the predicted rate separation. Together, our results suggest that discrete diffusion models learn data support before data frequencies.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 Dywave 动态分词框架，利用基于小波的层次化分解技术识别对应物理事件的语义时间边界，并对冗余时间间隔进行自适应压缩，从而构建出紧凑且保持时间一致性的输入表示。

Abstract: Internet of Things (IoT) systems continuously collect heterogeneous sensing signals from ubiquitous sensors to support intelligent applications such as human activity analysis, emotion monitoring, and environmental perception. These signals are inherently non-stationary and multi-scale, posing unique challenges for standard tokenization techniques. This paper proposes Dywave, a dynamic tokenization framework for IoT sensing signals that constructs compact input representations aligned with intrinsic temporal structures and underlying physical events. Dywave leverages wavelet-based hierarchical decomposition, identifies meaningful temporal boundaries corresponding to underlying semantic events, and adaptively compresses redundant intervals while preserving temporal coherence. Extensive evaluations on five real-world IoT sensing datasets across activity recognition, stress assessment, and nearby object detection demonstrate that Dywave outperforms state-of-the-art methods by up to 12% in accuracy, while improving computational efficiency by reducing input token lengths by up to 75% across mainstream sequence models. Moreover, Dywave exhibits improved robustness to domain shifts and varying sequence lengths.

### [141] [R2R2: Robust Representation for Intensive Experience Reuse via Redundancy Reduction in Self-Predictive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14026)
*Sanghyeob Song,Donghyeok Lee,Jinsik Kim,Sungroh Yoon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对高频率数据重用导致的强化学习过拟合问题，本文提出了 R2R2 正则化方法，通过修正 SPL 中的表征不稳定性，显著提升了机器人在数据稀缺环境下的学习效率与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数据稀缺的机器人领域，高更新比（UTD）虽然能提高数据利用效率，但也容易导致过拟合。现有研究多关注评价者（critic）的偏差，而对自预测学习（SPL）中表征层面的不稳定性研究不足，本文旨在解决这一问题。

Method: 作者提出了“通过冗余减少实现鲁棒表征”（R2R2）的正则化方法。该方法在理论上分析了标准零中心化处理与 SPL 频谱特性的冲突，进而设计了一个非中心化的优化目标，旨在提升高 UTD 状态下的模型稳定性。同时，作者通过将 SPL 模块整合进 SimbaV2，验证了该方法的通用性。

Result: 在 11 项连续控制任务中，R2R2 方法表现优异，在 UTD 比率为 20 时，使 TD7 的性能提升了约 22%；此外，R2R2 在 SimbaV2-SPL 上进一步带来了性能增益，使其达到了新的业内最高水平（SOTA）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 R2R2 方法通过引入非中心化目标函数，有效解决了自预测学习（SPL）在高数据更新比（UTD）机制下表征不稳定的问题，显著缓解了强化学习中的过拟合，并为提升数据效率提供了新的稳健表征学习范式。

Abstract: For reinforcement learning in data-scarce domains like real-world robotics, intensive data reuse enhances efficiency but induces overfitting. While prior works focus on critic bias, representation-level instability in Self-Predictive Learning (SPL) under high Update-to-Data (UTD) regimes remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method within SPL. We theoretically identify that standard zero-centering conflicts with SPL's spectral properties and design a non-centered objective accordingly. We verify R2R2 on SPL-native algorithms like TD7. Furthermore, to demonstrate its orthogonality to prior advancements, we extend the state-of-the-art SimbaV2, which originally lacks SPL, by integrating a tailored SPL module, termed SimbaV2-SPL. Experiments across 11 continuous control tasks confirm that R2R2 effectively mitigates overfitting; specifically, at a UTD ratio of 20, it improves TD7 by ~22% and provides additional gains on top of SimbaV2-SPL, which itself establishes a new state-of-the-art. The code can be found at: https://github.com/songsang7/R2R2

</details>


### [142] [Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention: Learning When to Write by Predicting Future Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14037)
*Gergely Szilvasy,Manuel Faysse,Maria Lomeli,Matthijs Douze,Pierre-Emmanuel Mazaré,Loïc Cabannes,Wen-tau Yih,Hervé Jégou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SP-KV 机制，通过轻量级效用预测器动态修剪 KV 缓存，在不牺牲模型性能的前提下大幅降低了长文本生成的显存需求和延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大模型处理长序列需求增加，Transformer 架构中 KV 缓存的内存占用和带宽瓶颈严重限制了生成效率。现有的方法往往难以在性能损耗与内存压缩之间取得平衡。

Method: 提出了一种自修剪键值注意力（Self-Pruned KV Attention, SP-KV）机制。通过引入一个轻量级的效用预测器，对 KV 对进行评分；采用保留局部窗口完整性与动态修剪旧 KV 对的策略，并与 LLM 进行端到端联合训练。

Result: SP-KV 能够实现 3 到 10 倍的 KV 缓存压缩率，且对验证损失和下游任务性能几乎没有影响。此外，该方法还揭示了模型层级和头级别的结构化稀疏模式。

Conclusion: SP-KV 是一种高效且灵活的 KV 缓存压缩技术，通过动态稀疏化在保持模型性能的同时，显著降低了长序列生成任务中的内存占用和延迟，并为架构设计提供了有价值的稀疏性洞察。

Abstract: Under modern test-time compute and agentic paradigms, language models process ever-longer sequences. Efficient text generation with transformer architectures is increasingly constrained by the Key-Value cache memory footprint and bandwidth. To address this limitation, we introduce Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV), a mechanism designed to predict future KV utility in order to reduce the size of the long-term KV cache. This strategy operates at a fine granularity: a lightweight utility predictor scores each key-value pair, and while recent KVs are always available via a local window, older pairs are written in the cache and used in global attention only if their predicted utility surpasses a given threshold. The LLM and the utility predictor are trained jointly end-to-end exclusively through next-token prediction loss, and are adapted from pretrained LLM checkpoints.
  Rather than enforcing a fixed compression ratio, SP-KV performs dynamic sparsification: the mechanism adapts to the input and typically reduces the KV cache size by a factor of $3$ to $10\times$, longer sequences often being more compressible. This leads to vast improvements in memory usage and decoding speed, with little to no degradation of validation loss nor performance on a broad set of downstream tasks. Beyond serving as an effective KV-cache reduction mechanism, our method reveals structured layer- and head-specific sparsity patterns that we can use to guide the design of hybrid local-global attention architectures.

### [143] [Reliability-Gated Source Anchoring for Continual Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14063)
*Vikash Singh,Debargha Ganguly,Weicong Chen,Sabyasachi Sahoo,Sreehari Sankar,Biyao Zhang,Mohsen Harir,Shouren Wang,Osama Zafar,Christian Gagné,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对持续测试时适应中因源模型失效导致的“盲目锚定”问题，本文提出了RMemSafe方法，通过引入基于熵的可靠性门控机制，动态屏蔽不可靠的源信息，实现了更具鲁棒性的适应效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在持续测试时适应（CTTA）任务中，现有的基于源锚定的方法假设预训练源模型始终保持一定的可靠性。然而，当面对极端数据腐蚀（如CCC-Hard数据集）时，源模型的准确率会急剧下降，此时继续强制锚定会导致“盲目锚定”失效，损害模型的适应性能。因此，需要一种能够动态判断并根据源模型可靠性调整锚定强度的机制。

Method: RMemSafe方法：1. 监测机制：利用冻结源模型的归一化预测熵来评估其在当前任务下的可靠性；2. 可靠性门控：当源模型预测趋于均匀分布（即不可靠）时，自动关闭源锚点及一致性过滤器；3. 后备策略：在门控关闭后，转而采用源不可知策略，结合基础损失函数和边际校准进行优化；4. 协同优化：与ASR（自动源重置）结合，在极端数据腐蚀下实现更优的鲁棒性。

Result: 在CCC-Hard数据集的9个连续腐蚀单元中，RMemSafe在8个单元上取得了最低错误率；作为重置类方法，其在所有9个单元上表现最佳；在ResNet-50和ViT-B/16上相比原有ROID+ASR方法分别提升了1.05个百分点和0.48个百分点；实验证明其受损曲线比原有方法更为平缓，体现了性能的平稳衰减。

Conclusion: 本文提出了RMemSafe，这是一种可靠性门控的持续测试时适应方法。通过引入基于源模型熵的门控机制，RMemSafe有效地解决了“盲目锚定”问题，在源模型不可靠时自动切换至源不可知模式，从而在持续漂移的数据流中实现了更稳健、更高精度的模型适应。

Abstract: Continual test-time adaptation (CTTA) updates a pretrained model online on an unlabeled, non-stationary stream while anchoring it to a frozen source checkpoint. This anchor is useful only when the source remains reliable. On CCC-Hard, however, a ResNet-50 source falls to approximately $1.3\%$ top-$1$ accuracy, while existing source-anchored CTTA methods continue applying the same anchor strength. We call this failure mode blind anchoring and propose RMemSafe, a reliability-gated extension of ROID that uses the frozen source's normalized predictive entropy to attenuate all explicit source-coupled uses in the objective. When the source posterior approaches uniformity, the gate closes: the source anchor and agreement filter vanish, and the objective reduces to a source-agnostic fallback comprising ROID's base losses plus marginal calibration. Combined with ASR, RMemSafe achieves the lowest error on $8$ of $9$ matched-split continual-corruption cells and is the best reset-based method on all $9$, improving ROID+ASR by $1.05$~pp on ResNet-50 and $0.48$~pp on ViT-B/16. A controlled source-degradation sweep shows a $1.13{\times}$ shallower harm slope than ROID+ASR, consistent with the graceful-decay prediction. The entropy gate detects high-entropy source collapse, not confidently wrong low-entropy sources; this scope is explicitly evaluated and discussed.

</details>


### [144] [SurF: A Generative Model for Multivariate Irregular Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14069)
*Mohammad R. Rezaei,Tejas Balaji,Rahul G. Krishnan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对不规则采样事件流建模难的问题，本文提出 SurF 模型，利用时间重标度定理实现了高效的生成建模，并构建了面向异步事件流的基础模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成模型在处理不规则采样的多元事件流时存在瓶颈：基于分词的方法难以应对跨度巨大的事件间隔，而神经时序点过程方法受限于窗口级的数值积分效率。

Method: 1. 提出 SurF 模型，利用时间重标度定理（TRT）构建事件序列与独立同分布（i.i.d.）单位速率指数噪声之间的可学习双射；2. 设计了三种可扩展至长序列的高效累积强度函数参数化方案；3. 引入基于 Transformer 的编码器，支持多数据集预训练。

Result: 在六个真实世界基准测试中，SurF 在 Earthquake、Retweet 和 Taobao 数据集上实现了最优的时间均方根误差（RMSE）；在严格的留一法验证协议下，SurF 在 5/6 的数据集上击败了所有经典及神经自回归基准模型，并在 Amazon 和 Earthquake 数据集上表现最优。

Conclusion: SurF 模型通过利用时间重标度定理，成功实现了对不规则采样多元事件流的统一建模，展现了作为异步事件流基础模型的潜力，在多个基准测试中超越了现有基准。

Abstract: Irregularly sampled multivariate event streams remain a stubbornly difficult modality for generative modeling: tokenization-based approaches break down when inter-event intervals vary by orders of magnitude, and neural temporal point processes are bottlenecked by window-level numerical quadrature. We (i) propose SurF, a generative model that uses the Time Rescaling Theorem (TRT) as a learnable bijection between event sequences and i.i.d.\ unit-rate exponential noise, enabling a single model to be trained across heterogeneous event-stream datasets; (ii) three efficient parameterizations of the cumulative intensity that scale to long sequences; and (iii) a Transformer-based encoder for multi-dataset pretraining. On six real-world benchmarks, SurF achieves the best reported time RMSE on Earthquake, Retweet, and Taobao, and is within trial-level noise of the strongest specialist on the remaining three. Under a strict leave-one-out protocol, the held-out checkpoint beats every classical and neural-autoregressive baseline on 5/6 datasets and beats every baseline on Amazon and Earthquake, an initial step toward foundation models over asynchronous event streams.

### [145] [Fair and Calibrated Toxicity Detection with Robust Training and Abstention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14074)
*Mokshit Surana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 毒性分类中的公平性不能仅看模型排名能力。研究发现，训练干预和事后安全措施（如校准和弃权）会产生意想不到的“校准失衡”，且不同方法的失败模式迥异，因此必须采用涵盖排序、校准和弃权的多维度评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前毒性分类的公平性研究往往将排序、校准和弃权割裂开来。作者旨在探讨训练时干预措施与事后安全机制之间的相互作用，并揭示现有方法如何导致隐藏的公平性失调。

Method: 作者对比了经验风险最小化（ERM）、实例级加权和组分布鲁棒优化（Group DRO）三种训练方法，并结合了温度缩放、基于置信度的弃权和按身份阈值优化等事后处理手段。通过子组AUC、BPSN/BNSP AUC、误差差距以及按子组期望校准误差（ECE）进行联合评估。

Result: 1. 校准差异是隐蔽的公平性违规，ERM在聚合层面表现良好但群体间差异大；2. 训练干预（如重加权）虽改善排序但恶化了校准差异，Group DRO虽平衡了校准但降低了整体性能；3. 事后修正方法在面对非均匀误校准时失效；4. 弃权机制本身存在偏见，对特定内容（背景内容）的覆盖效果远优于涉及身份的内容。

Conclusion: 毒性分类中的公平性需要多维评估框架（排序、校准和弃权）。仅关注聚合指标（如AUC）会掩盖不同身份群体在校准和弃权机制上的严重不平等。研究强调，训练干预和事后安全机制必须联合评估，因为它们之间存在复杂的权衡关系。

Abstract: Fairness in toxicity classification involves three integrated axes: ranking, calibration, and abstention. Training-time interventions and post-hoc safety mechanisms cannot be evaluated independently because the former determines the efficacy of the latter. We compare Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM), instance-level reweighting, and Group DRO across these axes, combined with temperature scaling, confidence-based abstention, and per-identity threshold optimization. Evaluation uses subgroup AUC, BPSN/BNSP AUC, error gaps, and per-subgroup Expected Calibration Error (ECE) with bootstrap CIs ($n = 1000$).
  We report four findings. (1) Calibration disparity is a hidden fairness violation. ERM has near-perfect aggregate calibration ($0.013$) but is significantly miscalibrated across all identity subgroups ($+0.029$ to $+0.134$). (2) Training interventions reshape rather than eliminate disparity. Reweighted ERM improves ranking (BPSN AUC $+0.06$ to $+0.12$) but worsens the calibration-fairness gap by up to $+0.232$. Group DRO eliminates calibration disparity but only by becoming uniformly miscalibrated globally (ECE $0.118$). (3) Post-hoc methods inherit training failure modes. Temperature scaling fails because miscalibration is non-uniform. Confidence-based abstention works under ERM but breaks under DRO, where the risk-coverage curve rises with deferral. (4) Abstention itself is unfair. Confidence-based deferral helps background content far more than identity-mentioning content. We argue that SRAI fairness requires a multi-axis framework: methods that differ only in aggregate ranking can differ sharply in failure modes that determine real-world harm.

Motivation: 分数匹配虽在学习连续指数族分布方面计算便捷且应用广泛，但其统计性质缺乏严谨的理论支持，尤其是缺乏非渐近样本复杂度的界限。

Result: 研究证明了分数匹配学习多项式指数族的样本复杂度与模型维度呈多项式依赖关系，打破了以往仅存在渐近性分析的局限。

Conclusion: 本文首次为分数匹配学习多项式指数族提供了非渐近样本复杂度界，证明了该方法在学习高维分布结构方面的有效性和理论上的优越性。

Abstract: Learning of continuous exponential family distributions with unbounded support remains an important area of research for both theory and applications in high-dimensional statistics. In recent years, score matching has become a widely used method for learning exponential families with continuous variables due to its computational ease when compared against maximum likelihood estimation. However, theoretical understanding of the statistical properties of score matching is still lacking. In this work, we provide a non-asymptotic sample complexity analysis for learning the structure of exponential families of polynomials with score matching. The derived sample bounds show a polynomial dependence on the model dimension. These bounds are the first of its kind, as all prior work has shown only asymptotic bounds on the sample complexity.

</details>


### [150] [CSI-JEPA: Towards Foundation Representations for Ubiquitous Sensing with Minimal Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14171)
*Xuanhao Luo,Zhizhen Li,Yuchen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CSI-JEPA 是一种针对 Wi-Fi 感知的自监督表征学习框架，通过预测掩码信道特征，实现了高效的标签利用，在多任务感知中显著提升了性能并大幅降低了标注成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 CSI 感知模型极度依赖大量标注数据，在面临不同任务、设备或环境变化时，标注成本高昂且难以扩展。为了解决这一痛点，需要利用海量的无标签 CSI 数据进行高效的表征学习。

Method: 提出 CSI-JEPA 框架：1) 采用基于掩码的自监督预测学习，通过可见上下文预测隐藏区域的潜在特征；2) 针对 CSI 的物理特性，在时间和子载波维度进行分块（Tokenization）；3) 引入“信道变化感知”的掩码策略，优先采样高动态变化的区域；4) 预训练后冻结编码器，仅通过轻量级适配器处理下游任务。

Result: 在七个真实 Wi-Fi 感知任务上进行了测试，结果显示 CSI-JEPA 相比现有的监督学习 Transformer 模型，平均准确率提升了 10.64 个百分点，且在同等预算下，标签需求量最高可减少 98%。

Conclusion: CSI-JEPA 通过自监督学习成功提取了通用的 CSI 时频表征，证明了该方法在减少标签依赖的同时，能够显著提升多种 Wi-Fi 感知任务的性能，是解决 CSI 感知领域数据匮乏与多任务迁移问题的有效途径。

Abstract: Channel state information (CSI) provides a widely available sensing modality for human and environment perception, but existing CSI sensing models usually rely on task-specific supervised training and require substantial labeled data for each task, device, user, or environment. This limits their scalability in practical deployments where unlabeled CSI is abundant but labeled data is costly to collect. In this paper, we present CSI-JEPA, a self-supervised predictive representation learning framework for label-efficient, multi-task Wi-Fi sensing. CSI-JEPA learns reusable temporal-spectral representations from unlabeled CSI samples by predicting latent features of masked channel regions from visible context. To better match the physical structure of CSI, CSI-JEPA tokenizes channel-response amplitude windows along the time and subcarrier dimensions. It then introduces a channel variation-aware masking strategy that samples predictive targets from regions with stronger local temporal and subcarrier-domain variations. After pretraining, the encoder is frozen and used as a backbone, with lightweight task-specific adapters added for downstream sensing tasks. We evaluate CSI-JEPA on seven real-world Wi-Fi sensing tasks spanning diverse objectives and deployment settings. The results show that CSI-JEPA improves downstream sensing performance over competitive baselines, achieving up to 10.64 percentage points mean accuracy gain over state-of-the-art supervised Transformer and matched-budget label savings of up to 98.0%.

### [151] [LLMs Know When They Know, but Do Not Act on It: A Metacognitive Harness for Test-time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14186)
*Qi Cao,Yufan Wang,Peijia Qin,Shuhao Zhang,Pengtao Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为“元认知控制框架”的方法，通过将大模型的自我评估信号（推理前后的知晓感与学习判断）转化为推理过程的控制指令，在无需训练的情况下显著增强了模型在文本、代码及多模态任务中的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在推理前后表现出了一定的自我监控能力（如评估成功率或答案正确性），但这些信号通常被孤立地测量，未能有效应用于推理过程的控制。研究者旨在探索这些潜在的元认知能力是否可以转化为有效的测试时控制手段。

Method: 受认知心理学中Nelson-Narens理论的启发，作者提出了一种“元认知控制框架（metacognitive harness）”。该框架将模型的自我监控与推理过程分离，具体包括：在推理前报告“知晓感（FOK）”，并在推理后报告“学习判断（JOL）”。这些信号不再被视为被动的置信度估计，而是转化为明确的推理控制界面，用于决定何时信任当前解、何时利用反馈进行重试以及何时将多个尝试交给聚合器。

Result: 在无需参数更新或特定任务微调的情况下，该方法大幅提升了Claude Sonnet-4.6的基础性能。在HLE-Verified、LiveCodeBench v6和R-Bench-V等基准测试中，模型整体准确率从48.3%提升至56.9%，并在多个核心评估设置中超过了排行榜上的现有最高纪录。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型（LLMs）确实具备潜在的元认知能力，但这种能力需要通过明确的“元认知控制框架”才能在推理过程中被有效激发和利用，从而显著提升模型的性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often expose useful signals of self-monitoring: before solving a problem, they can estimate whether they are likely to succeed, and after solving it, they can judge whether their answer is likely to be correct. However, these signals are typically measured or elicited in isolation, rather than used to control inference. In this work, we ask whether LLMs possess latent metacognitive ability that can be turned into effective test-time control. Inspired by the Nelson--Narens theory from cognitive psychology, we propose a metacognitive harness that separates monitoring from reasoning. For each problem, the model first reports a pre-solve feeling-of-knowing (FOK) signal; after each solve attempt, it reports a post-solve judgment-of-learning (JOL) signal. Rather than treating these signals as passive confidence estimates, the harness turns them into an explicit control interface for reasoning: it decides when to trust the current solution, when to retry with compact metacognitive feedback, and when to pass multiple attempts to a final aggregator. Across text, code, and multimodal reasoning benchmarks, our harness substantially improves a fixed Claude Sonnet-4.6 base model without parameter updates or benchmark-specific fine-tuning. On the evaluated public benchmark snapshots, it raises pooled accuracy from 48.3 to 56.9 and exceeds the strongest listed leaderboard entries on the three primary evaluation settings: HLE-Verified, LiveCodeBench v6, and R-Bench-V. These results suggest that strong LLMs may already possess useful metacognitive ability, but require an explicit control harness to act on it during reasoning.

</details>

*Yingying Fang,Haijie Xu,Shuang Wu,Mariathasan Anish,Guang Yang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种细粒度概念瓶颈模型（Fine-grained CBM）框架。该方法强制将每个概念“扎根”（grounding）在局部化的视觉证据中，通过这种空间对齐机制，使用户能够直接观察并验证模型是如何识别概念的，从而区分出模型学习的是真实特征还是虚假相关性。

Result: 在医学影像基准测试中，该方法构建的概念空间信息完整，其预测性能与标准CBM相当，同时在透明度和概念表征的正确性验证方面有显著提升，优于传统的后验归因方法。

Conclusion: 该框架通过将概念定位到具体的视觉证据，解决了传统概念瓶颈模型（CBM）缺乏可验证性的问题。它在保持高性能的同时，显著提升了模型透明度和可信度，为医疗影像等高风险领域提供了更具实操性的可解释学习方案。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) offer interpretable alternatives to black-box predictors by introducing human-relatable concepts before the final output. However, existing CBMs struggle to verify whether predicted concepts correspond to the correct visual evidence, limiting their reliability. We propose a fine-grained CBM framework that grounds each concept in localized visual evidence, enabling direct inspection of where and how concepts are encoded. This design allows users to interpret predictions and verify that the model learns intended concepts rather than spurious correlations. Experiments on medical imaging benchmarks show that our learned concept space is information-complete and achieves predictive performance comparable to standard CBMs, while substantially improving transparency. Unlike post-hoc attribution methods, our framework validates both the presence and correctness of concept representations, bridging interpretability with verifiability. Our approach enhances the trustworthiness of CBMs and establishes a principled mechanism for human-model interaction at the concept level, paving the way toward more reliable and clinically actionable concept-based learning systems.

### [153] [PreFT: Prefill-only finetuning for efficient inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14217)
*Andrew Lanpouthakoun,Aryaman Arora,Zhengxuan Wu,Dhruv Pai,Ben Keigwin,Dan Jurafsky,Christopher Potts*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为PreFT的新型微调方法，通过仅在推理的“预填充”阶段使用适配器，绕过了多适配器在“解码”阶段带来的性能瓶颈，显著提升了大规模个性化大模型的服务吞吐量，且性能损失极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模个性化场景中，现有的参数高效微调（PEFT）方法在多用户同时部署时会严重降低推理服务的吞吐量，尤其是在解码阶段。现有研究过度关注参数数量的优化，而忽略了在多适配器并发服务场景下对系统吞吐量的优化。

Method: 论文提出了“仅预填充微调”（PreFT）方法，即仅在预填充（Prefill）阶段应用适配器（如LoRA和ReFT），而在随后的解码（Decode）阶段舍弃适配器。作者基于vLLM推理引擎实现了该方法，并通过增加适配器秩（rank）的方式来弥补仅在预填充阶段应用带来的性能损耗。

Result: 实验结果显示，在Llama 3.1 70B模型上，使用PreFT服务512个适配器的吞吐量是传统PEFT方法的1.9倍。在监督微调（SFT）任务中，虽然PreFT的评估损失略高，但可通过提升适配器秩来补偿；在强化学习（RL）任务中，PreFT的效果与标准PEFT几乎持平。

Conclusion: 研究表明，仅针对预填充阶段进行适配器微调（PreFT）是一种更优的个性化大模型部署策略。它在保持与传统全阶段微调相当的性能的同时，显著提升了多用户场景下的服务吞吐量，为大规模个性化部署提供了更好的准确率-吞吐量权衡方案。

Abstract: Large language models can now be personalised efficiently at scale using parameter efficient finetuning methods (PEFTs), but serving user-specific PEFTs harms throughput, even with specialised kernels and memory management techniques. This is because, theoretically and empirically, a mismatch exists between prefill (processing a large number of tokens at once) and decode (generating a single token autoregressively): the latter has far lower throughput when serving multiple adapters. Rather than optimising performance relative to parameter count, for efficient multi-adapter serving, we instead ought to optimise performance relative to serving throughput. We therefore propose PreFT (Prefill-only Finetuning), wherein we only apply the adapter to prefill tokens and discard it afterwards. PreFT significantly increases throughput with minimal effect on performance. We develop and release an efficient implementation of two prefill-only PEFTs, LoRA and ReFT, on the vLLM inference engine. We first show that serving multi-user PreFTs is more efficient than traditional PEFTs ($1.9\times$ the throughput when serving $512$ adapters on Llama 3.1 70B). Then, we compare the performance of prefill-only vs. all-token adapters on a variety of supervised finetuning and reinforcement learning tasks with LMs at varying scales. On SFT, we observe that the evaluation loss of PreFTs is higher than PEFTs, but can be compensated by increasing rank with nearly no reduction in throughput. On RL, we consistently find that PreFTs approach parity with standard PEFTs. Together, this work validates prefill-only adaptation of LLMs as a more favourable accuracy-throughput tradeoff than existing PEFTs for personalised serving.

</details>


### [154] [Diagnosing Training Inference Mismatch in LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14220)
*Tianle Zhong,Neiwen Ling,Yifan Pi,Zijun Wei,Tianshu Yu,Geoffrey Fox,Peng Wu,Xiao Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了LLM强化学习中“训练-推理不匹配（TIM）”现象的危害，证明了即使微小的数值差异也足以导致训练崩溃，并提出了相应的缓解策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM强化学习系统常将采样生成与策略优化分离，导致即使模型权重相同，两个阶段仍可能产生不同的Token概率。这种“训练-推理不匹配（TIM）”现象极易被掩盖，且其对模型稳定性的影响机制尚不明确。

Method: 作者设计了零不匹配诊断框架（VeXact），通过隔离其他变量（如离策略漂移等），定量研究了微小的Token级数值差异如何独立导致训练崩溃，并提出了一系列针对性的缓解措施。

Result: 研究发现，即使是微小的数值差异也会诱发严重的训练崩溃。TIM实际上改变了优化问题的本质，其影响不容忽视。

Conclusion: 训练-推理不匹配（TIM）并非无害的数值噪声，而是导致LLM强化学习训练不稳定的关键系统级扰动因素，在模型分析与训练中应作为首要考量。

Abstract: Modern LLM RL systems separate rollout generation from policy optimization. These two stages are expected to produce token probabilities that match exactly. However, implementation differences can make them assign different values to the same sequence under the same model weights, inducing Training-Inference Mismatch (TIM). TIM is difficult to inspect because it is entangled with off-policy drift and common stabilization mechanisms. In this work, we isolate TIM in a zero-mismatch diagnostic setting (VeXact), and show that small token-level numerical disagreements can independently cause training collapse. We further show that TIM changes the effective optimization problem, and identify a set of remedies that could mitigate TIM. Our results suggest that TIM is not benign numerical noise, but a systems-level perturbation that should be treated as a first-order factor in analyzing LLM RL stability.

This highlights the importance of leveraging large, multi-hospital health systems for training and validation to better reflect real-world clinical complexity. In this work, we develop DT-Transformer, a foundation model trained on 57.1M structured EHR entries over 1.7M patients from Mass General Brigham (MGB), spanning 11 hospitals and a broad network of outpatient clinics. DT-Transformer achieves strong discrimination in both held-out and prospective validation settings. Next-event prediction achieves a median age- and sex-stratified AUC of 0.871 across 896 disease categories, with all categories exceeding AUC 0.5. These results support health system-scale training as a path toward foundation models suited to real-world clinical forecasting.

### [156] [AudioMosaic: Contrastive Masked Audio Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14231)
*Hanxun Huang,Qizhou Wang,Xingjun Ma,Cihang Xie,Christopher Leckie,Sarah Erfani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AudioMosaic 是一种新型对比学习音频编码器，通过结构化时频掩码构建正样本，高效学习通用音频表征，在多项基准测试中实现 SOTA，并能有效赋能音频-语言任务。
