Method: 提出了一种名为 AudioMosaic 的对比学习音频编码器。其核心创新在于采用结构化的时频掩码技术（Structured Time-Frequency Masking）来构建正样本对，无需依赖复杂的音频增强，从而有效降低了计算内存消耗，实现了高效的大批量预训练。

Result: 实验表明，AudioMosaic 在多个标准音频基准测试中在线性探测和微调设置下均达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能。此外，将其集成到音频-语言模型中，显著提升了音频-语言相关任务的效果。

Conclusion: AudioMosaic 证明了基于对比学习的方法在音频自监督学习中具有优越性。通过创新的结构化时频掩码技术，该模型不仅提高了预训练效率，还增强了特征的判别力。研究表明，该编码器在多种音频任务及音频-语言模型中具有极强的迁移能力和通用性，为音频表征学习提供了新的高效范式。

Abstract: Audio self-supervised learning (SSL) aims to learn general-purpose representations from large-scale unlabeled audio data. While recent advances have been driven mainly by generative reconstruction objectives, contrastive approaches remain less explored, partly due to the difficulty of designing effective audio augmentations and the large batch sizes required for contrastive pre-training. We introduce \textbf{AudioMosaic}, a contrastive learning-based audio encoder for general audio understanding. During pre-training, AudioMosaic constructs positive pairs by applying structured time-frequency masking to spectrogram patches, which reduces memory usage and enables efficient large-batch training. Compared with generative approaches, the AudioMosaic encoder learns more discriminative utterance-level representations that demonstrate strong transferability across datasets, domains, and acoustic conditions. Extensive experiments show that AudioMosaic achieves state-of-the-art performance on several standard audio benchmarks under both linear probing and fine-tuning. We further show that integrating the pretrained AudioMosaic encoder into audio-language models improves performance on audio-language tasks. The code is publicly available in our \href{https://github.com/HanxunH/AudioMosaic}{GitHub repository}.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前量子多智能体强化学习（QMARL）研究缺乏可证明的基准，难以区分量子优势与算法巧合。因此，研究旨在通过数学上可证明的基准任务（如CHSH博弈）来严格评估量子纠缠在多智能体协同中的实际作用，并验证量子优势的来源。

Method: 研究采用了基于变分量子电路（VQC）的分布式QMARL框架，并引入了共享纠缠态机制。实验设计包括：1. 在CHSH博弈中测试量子纠缠对协调任务的影响，并与经典性能上限（0.75）进行对比；2. 在CoopNav任务中，将QMARL架构与经典MAA2C算法进行对比，并评估了不同纠缠结构的效果。

Result: 1. 在CHSH博弈中，具有纠缠态的智能体胜率达到了约0.854（接近Tsirelson界限），超过了经典上限0.75，而未纠缠的量子电路表现仅与经典基准相当；2. 在CoopNav任务中，无纠缠的QMARL成功率约为0.85，是经典MAA2C（0.40）的两倍；3. 混合架构（量子执行器+经典中心化评价器）在性能上表现最优。

Conclusion: 本文通过实证研究证明，量子纠缠是实现多智能体协同优势的关键机制。在CHSH博弈中，纠缠态使智能体突破了经典上限，达到了Tsirelson界限。此外，混合架构（量子执行器+经典中心化评价器）在复杂任务中表现出优于纯量子或纯经典模型的协同能力，为QMARL的未来设计提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We present an empirical evaluation of quantum entanglement in agent coordination within quantum multi agent reinforcement learning (QMARL). While QMARL has attracted growing interest recently, most prior work evaluates quantum policies without provable baselines, making it impossible to rigorously distinguish quantum advantage from algorithmic coincidence. We address this directly by evaluating a decentralized QMARL framework with variational quantum circuit (VQC) actors with shared entangled states. In the CHSH game, which has a mathematically proven classical performance ceiling of 0.75 win rate, we show that entangled QMARL agents approach the Tsirelson limit of 0.854, providing clear evidence of their quantum advantage. We show that unentangled quantum circuits match the classical baseline, confirming that entanglement and not the quantum circuit itself is the active coordination mechanism. We also explore the effect of specific entanglement structures, as some Bell states enable coordination gains while others actively harm performance. On cooperative navigation (CoopNav), QMARL without entanglement achieves $\sim2\times$ improvement in success rate over classical MAA2C ($\sim$0.85 versus $\sim$0.40), with the hybrid configuration, quantum actor paired with a classical centralised critic, outperforming both fully classical and fully quantum solutions. We present our experimental analysis and discuss future work.

### [158] [Active Learners as Efficient PRP Rerankers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14236)
*Jeremías Figueiredo Paschmann,Juan Kaplan,Francisco Nattero Santiago Mauricio Barron Bucolo,Juan Wisznia,Luciano del Corro*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的成对排序（PRP）方法通常依赖于经典排序算法，但LLM输出的偏好判断往往存在噪声、对顺序敏感且存在非传递性，这导致基于完美排序假设的算法在有限的调用预算下难以获得可靠的Top-K排序结果。

Method: 1. 将Pairwise Ranking Prompting (PRP)重新建模为从带噪声的成对比较中进行主动学习；
2. 引入主动排序算法替代传统的排序算法，以适应资源约束环境；
3. 开发了一种随机方向预言机（randomized-direction oracle），仅需单次大模型调用即可完成成对比较，将系统性位置偏差转化为零均值噪声。

Result: 该方法在调用受限的情况下，显著提升了NDCG@10指标，并证明了其作为现有排序流程的“即插即用”式替代方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于主动学习的排序框架，通过将成对偏好排序任务转化为带噪声的主动学习问题，在资源受限的情况下显著优于传统的排序算法，并有效降低了位置偏差的影响。

Abstract: Pairwise Ranking Prompting (PRP) elicits pairwise preference judgments from an LLM, which are then aggregated into a ranking, usually via classical sorting algorithms. However, judgments are noisy, order-sensitive, and sometimes intransitive, so sorting assumptions do not match the setting. Because sorting aims to recover a full permutation, truncating it to meet a call budget does not produce a dependable top-K. We thus reframe PRP reranking as active learning from noisy pairwise comparisons and show that active rankers are drop-in replacements that improve NDCG@10 per call in the call-constrained regime. Our noise-robust framework also introduces a randomized-direction oracle that uses a single LLM call per pair. This approach converts systematic position bias into zero-mean noise, enabling unbiased aggregate ranking without the cost of bidirectional calls.

Abstract: The recent large-scale emergence of LLMs has left an open space for dealing with their consequences, such as plagiarism or the spread of false information on the Internet. Coupling this with the rise of AI detector bypassing tools, reliable machine-generated text detection is in increasingly high demand. We investigate the paraphrasing attack resilience of various machine-generated text detection methods, evaluating three approaches: fine-tuned RoBERTa, Binoculars, and text feature analysis, along with their ensembles using Random Forest classifiers. We discovered that Binoculars-inclusive ensembles yield the strongest results, but they also suffer the most significant losses during attacks. In this paper, we present the dichotomy of performance versus resilience in the world of AI text detection, which complicates the current perception of reliability among state-of-the-art techniques.

### [161] [Architecture-Aware Explanation Auditing for Industrial Visual Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14255)
*Sibo Jia,Zihang Zhao,Kunrong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个架构感知的解释审计协议，证明了模型内部“读取结构”决定了解释的真实有效性。研究指出，开发者不应仅依赖直观热图，而应协同设计解释器与模型结构，并辅以定量的忠实度指标以确保决策可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业视觉系统中，深度学习模型的解释热图（Heatmaps）常出现视觉上看起来合理，但实际上并未捕捉模型真实决策依据的情况（即缺乏忠实度）。现有研究缺乏对解释方法与模型架构内在读取机制之间适配性的定量审计框架。

Method: 提出了一套基于“原生读取假设”（native-readout hypothesis）的架构感知解释审计协议。该协议通过扰动测试（Deletion AUC）评估解释方法的忠实度，并利用结构距离指标衡量解释机制与模型内部决策机制的一致性。研究在WM-811K晶圆数据集上对比了多种架构（ViT、Swin、ResNet、DenseNet）与不同解释技术（Attention Rollout、Grad-CAM、RISE），并通过敏感性分析（改变扰动基准）与跨数据集（MVTec AD）验证了结果的鲁棒性。

Result: 研究发现：1) 解释的忠实度受模型读取结构影响巨大，并非所有架构都适合特定的解释方法；2) 即使是性能较差的模型，若其内部架构与解释器更匹配，也能提供更忠实的解释；3) 所谓“原生”解释方法并非总是最优，模型无关（model-agnostic）方法如RISE在特定条件下表现更佳；4) 忠实度排名是模型、解释器与扰动操作共同作用的结果，具有高度的依赖性。

Conclusion: 解释器的有效性（忠实度）不仅取决于模型本身，还受到解释方法与模型架构读取机制（readout structure）匹配程度的影响。研究强调在部署工业视觉解释系统时，必须协同设计模型架构与解释路径，并强制配套定量忠实度指标，以避免视觉上“合理”但实则误导的解释。

Abstract: Industrial visual inspection systems increasingly rely on deep classifiers whose heatmap explanations may appear visually plausible while failing to identify the image regions that actually drive model decisions. This paper operationalizes an architecture-aware explanation audit protocol grounded in the native-readout hypothesis: the perturbation-based faithfulness of an explanation method is bounded by its structural distance from the model's native decision mechanism. On WM-811K wafer maps (9 classes, 172k images) under a three-seed zero-fill perturbation protocol, ViT-Tiny + Attention Rollout attains Deletion AUC 0.211 against 0.432-0.525 for Swin-Tiny / ResNet18+CBAM / DenseNet121 + Grad-CAM (abs(Cohen's d) > 1.1), despite lower classification accuracy. Swin-Tiny disentangles architecture family from readout structure: despite being a Transformer, its spatial feature-map hierarchy makes it Grad-CAM compatible, showing that the operative factor is readout structure rather than architecture family. A model-agnostic control (RISE) compresses all families to Deletion AUC about 0.1, indicating the gap arises from the explainer pathway; notably, RISE outperforms all native methods, so native readout is a compatibility principle rather than an optimality guarantee. A blur-fill sensitivity analysis shows that the family ordering reverses under a different perturbation baseline, reinforcing that faithfulness rankings are joint properties of (model, explainer, perturbation operator) triples. An exploratory boundary-condition study on MVTec AD (pretrained models) indicates that audit results are dataset/task dependent and identifies conditions requiring qualification. The protocol yields actionable guidance: explanation pathways should be co-designed with model architectures based on readout structure, and deployed heatmaps should be accompanied by quantitative faithfulness metrics.

*Libo Sun,Po-wei Harn,Peixiong He,Xiao Qin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: KV-cache compression at small budgets is a crowded design space spanning cache representation, head-wise routing, compression cadence, decoding behavior, and within-budget scoring. All seven were rejected. We then propose $α$, a one-function modification to the TriAttention~\cite{mao2026triattention} retention scorer that replaces argmax-top-$k$ with greedy facility-location-inspired selection under a V-space redundancy penalty controlled by a single weight $λ$. A pre-registered protocol tunes $λ$ on a frozen development split and confirms on a disjoint held-out split; with $λ= 0.5$, $α$ clears Bonferroni on two of the four (model, budget) cells (Qwen $b{=}128$ and Llama $b{=}64$), no cell is significantly negative, and the pre-registered Branch~A triggers. The finding is asymmetric: a minimal scoring modification beat heavier structural redesigns in this regime, and the combined matched-memory, sympy-graded, held-out confirmation protocol is the evidence standard that made the asymmetry visible.

### [163] [Policy Optimization in Hybrid Discrete-Continuous Action Spaces via Mixed Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14297)
*Matias Alvo,Daniel Russo,Yash Kanoria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对混合离散-连续动作空间下的强化学习难题，本文提出了混合策略优化（HPO）算法。该方法通过结合路径导数与得分函数估计器，在保持梯度的无偏性的同时，显著提升了高维混合动作空间下的训练效果与收敛稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在混合离散-连续动作空间中，现有的无模型策略梯度方法（如PPO）在处理高维空间时面临严重的信用分配问题，导致梯度质量低下；而基于可微分模拟的方法又往往因为存在离散动作或动力学不可微，导致梯度有偏或信息不足。研究旨在解决这些方法在处理混合决策结构时的缺陷。

Method: 提出了一种混合策略优化（Hybrid Policy Optimization, HPO）算法。该方法结合了路径导数（pathwise gradients，用于利用模拟器信息）和得分函数（score-function，用于处理不连续性和离散动作）两种估计器，通过混合使用确保了梯度估计的无偏性，并利用可微分模拟技术在允许的平滑区域进行反向传播。此外，作者还提出了一种将动作不连续问题重构为混合形式的通用框架。

Result: 实验结果显示，HPO在库存控制和切换线性二次型调节器（LQR）等任务上显著优于PPO。随着连续动作维度的增加，HPO的性能优势进一步扩大。此外，理论分析揭示了混合梯度中交叉项（捕捉连续动作对未来离散决策的影响）在接近最优解时可忽略，证明了其在优化末期可进行近似解耦更新。

Conclusion: 本文提出的HPO方法通过结合路径导数和得分函数估计器，有效解决了混合动作空间中策略梯度的方差和偏差问题，特别是在高维连续控制场景下表现出显著的优越性和收敛效率。其理论分析表明，在接近最优解时，离散与连续动作的梯度更新可实现近似解耦，从而降低了计算复杂度和方差。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning in hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces, such as settings where the discrete component selects a regime (or index) and the continuous component optimizes within it -- a structure common in robotics, control, and operations problems. Standard model-free policy gradient methods rely on score-function (SF) estimators and suffer from severe credit-assignment issues in high-dimensional settings, leading to poor gradient quality. On the other hand, differentiable simulation largely sidesteps these issues by backpropagating through a simulator, but the presence of discrete actions or non-smooth dynamics yields biased or uninformative gradients. To address this, we propose Hybrid Policy Optimization (HPO), which backpropagates through the simulator wherever smoothness permits, using a mixed gradient estimator that combines pathwise and SF gradients while maintaining unbiasedness. We also show how problems with action discontinuities can be reformulated in hybrid form, further broadening its applicability. Empirically, HPO substantially outperforms PPO on inventory control and switched linear-quadratic regulator problems, with performance gaps increasing as the continuous action dimension grows. Finally, we characterize the structure of the mixed gradient, showing that its cross term -- which captures how continuous actions influence future discrete decisions -- becomes negligible near a discrete best response, thereby enabling approximate decentralized updates of the continuous and discrete components and reducing variance near optimality. All resources are available at github.com/MatiasAlvo/hybrid-rl.

</details>


### [164] [Language-Induced Priors for Domain Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14301)
*Qiyuan Chen,Jiayu Zhou,Raed Al Kontar*

TL;DR: 本文针对领域自适应冷启动问题，通过引入大模型生成的文本先验（LIP）来指导源域选择，有效解决了数据匮乏导致的负迁移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在领域自适应的冷启动场景下，由于目标数据匮乏，传统统计方法难以区分相关与无关的源域，导致负迁移现象严重。本文旨在利用通常被忽视的、关于目标领域的专家文本描述资源来解决这一挑战。

Method: 提出了一种“语言诱导先验（LIP）”框架，利用预训练大语言模型（LLM）处理目标领域的专家文本描述，将其转化为选择模型；并将该先验整合进期望最大化（EM）算法中，用于在目标数据稀缺时引导源域的选择，并随着数据积累逐步精炼选择。

Result: 理论上证明了该估计器在正确先验下接近预言机（oracle）的冷启动均方误差，并保证了无论先验质量如何都能达到渐近一致性；实证研究涵盖了高斯估计、预测性任务（C-MAPSS）和决策任务（MuJoCo hopper），均验证了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种将语言描述整合进领域自适应的新范式，证明了利用大模型先验可以在冷启动阶段有效缓解负迁移问题，且该框架具有良好的通用性和理论保障。

Abstract: Domain adaptation faces a fundamental paradox in the cold-start regime. When target data is scarce, statistical methods fail to distinguish relevant source domains from irrelevant ones, which often leads to negative transfer. In this paper, we address this challenge by leveraging expert textual descriptions of the target domain, a resource that is often available but overlooked. We propose a probabilistic framework that translates these semantic descriptions into a choice model, namely a Language-Induced Prior (LIP), that learns the preferences from a pretrained Large Language Model (LLM). The LIP is then integrated into an Expectation-Maximization algorithm to identify source relevance. Methodologically, this framework is compatible with any parametric model where a likelihood is available. It allows the LIP to guide the selection of sources when target signals are weak, while gradually refining these choices as samples accumulate. Theoretically, we prove that the estimator roughly matches an oracle cold-start MSE under a correct prior, while remaining asymptotically consistent regardless of the quality of the LIP. Empirically, we validated the framework on a descriptive (Gaussian estimation), a predictive (C-MAPSS dataset), and a prescriptive task (MuJoCo hopper).

</details>


### [165] [Matrix-Space Reinforcement Learning for Reusing Local Transition Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14304)
*Zuyuan Zhang,Carlee Joe-Wong,Tian Lan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有序列决策方法在处理组合泛化时，往往忽略了局部轨迹的几何结构与动力学特征，导致在跨任务迁移时无法有效识别并复用已有的有用知识。

Method: 提出“矩阵空间强化学习 (MSRL)”，将轨迹片段抽象为正半定矩阵描述符，聚合了一阶和二阶统计信息；利用该描述符的代数特性进行任务组合与迁移，并结合值函数条件化以及“阻碍过滤”机制，实现模型无关和模型基于算法的无缝集成。

Result: MSRL 在有限预算下的平均目标 AUC 达到 0.73，显著优于从零开始训练（0.65）、TD-MPC-PT+FT（0.63）以及 TD-MPC（0.57）等基准模型。

Conclusion: MSRL 框架通过引入矩阵空间抽象，成功将复杂轨迹分段映射为可代数组合的描述符，为强化学习中的组合泛化问题提供了一种高效的理论与实践方案。实验证明该方法在有限任务预算下显著提升了学习效率和策略迁移能力。

Abstract: Compositional generalization in sequential decision-making requires identifying which parts of prior rollouts remain useful for new tasks. Existing methods reuse skills or predictive models, but often overlook rich local transition geometry and dynamics. We propose Matrix-Space Reinforcement Learning (MSRL), a geometric abstraction that represents trajectory segments through positive semidefinite matrix descriptors aggregating first- and second-order statistics of lifted one-step transitions. These descriptors expose shared hidden structure, support algebraic composition in an abstract matrix space, and reveal opportunities for transfer. We prove that the descriptor is well defined up to coordinate gauge, complete for the induced low-order additive signal class, additive under valid segment composition, and minimally sufficient among admissible additive descriptors. We further show that conditioning value functions on the trajectory-segment matrix yields a first-order smooth approximation of action values, enabling source-learned matrix-to-value mappings to bootstrap learning in new tasks. MSRL is plug-in compatible with standard model-free and model-based methods, while obstruction filtering rejects implausible compositions. Empirically, MSRL achieves the best average finite-budget target AUC of 0.73, outperforming MSRL from scratch (0.65), TD-MPC-PT+FT (0.63), and TD-MPC (0.57).

Instead of directly perturbing atmospheric states, our method steers the diffusion sampling trajectory, enabling precipitation reduction while maintaining consistency with the atmospheric distribution. To assess physical plausibility, we evaluate from three perspectives: (i) vertical and variable-wise perturbation profiles, (ii) latent-space trajectory deviation, and (iii) cross-model transferability. ### [169] [Nearest-Neighbor Radii under Dependent Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14343)
*Yuanyuan Gao,Yilong Hou,Zhexiao Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了相依采样下最近邻半径的几何特性，证明了其与独立采样下的相似性，并推导了基于局部内蕴维数的非渐近界，从而证实了最近邻方法在处理时序等相依数据时的鲁棒性与有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的最近邻方法几何分析主要建立在独立同分布（i.i.d.）采样假设之上，但在实际应用中，数据往往存在时间或空间上的相依性。研究者希望探究这种相依性是否会改变最近邻邻域的尺度，以及在这种情况下最近邻方法是否仍然有效。

Method: 本文针对强混合（strong mixing）相依观测数据，在多项式混合条件下推导了最近邻半径的几乎处处收敛性（almost sure convergence），并在几何混合条件下导出了关于局部内蕴维数（local intrinsic dimension）的尖锐非渐近矩界（non-asymptotic moment bounds）。实验部分通过合成数据和真实世界的时间序列基准测试验证了上述理论结论。

Result: 研究结果表明，相依采样下的最近邻半径表现与独立采样相似。所导出的矩界取决于数据的局部内蕴维数而非环境维数，这意味着该方法能够有效处理嵌入在低维流形上的高维数据，且在理论和实证上均证实了最近邻几何结构在相依数据下的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了即使在相依采样下，最近邻几何特性（如邻域半径）依然是信息丰富的，且其表现与独立采样下的情况具有一致性。该理论为将最近邻方法应用于金融、气象等包含时序相依性的复杂高维数据提供了严谨的数学支撑。

Abstract: Nearest-neighbor methods are fundamental to classical and modern machine learning, yet their geometric properties are typically analyzed under independent sampling. In this paper, we study the nearest-neighbor radii under dependent sampling. We consider strong mixing dependent observations and ask whether dependence changes the scale of nearest-neighbor neighborhoods. We establish distribution-free almost sure convergence under polynomial mixing and sharp non-asymptotic moment bounds under geometric mixing. The moment bounds depend on the local intrinsic dimension rather than the ambient dimension, making the results applicable to high-dimensional data concentrated near lower-dimensional manifolds. Synthetic experiments and real-world time-series benchmarks support the theory, showing that nearest-neighbor geometry remains informative under dependence sampling.

### [170] [Exemplar Partitioning for Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14347)
*Jessica Rumbelow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的可解释性工具“示例划分”（EP），通过对模型激活空间进行几何聚类，用少量的真实示例替代昂贵的稀疏自编码器，实现了在极大降低计算成本的同时，获得具备可解释性、因果干预能力及跨模型可比性的特征字典。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的稀疏自编码器（SAE）在提取大语言模型可解释特征时需要消耗巨大的计算资源（海量标记数据）。为了解决这一问题，研究者旨在开发一种无需大量训练开销、能通过观测到的示例直接构建可解释特征字典，并支持跨模型、跨检查点比较的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“示例划分”（Exemplar Partitioning, EP）的方法，通过对流式模型激活值进行基于距离阈值的领导者聚类（Leader-clustering），构建出以观测到的真实示例为锚点的Voronoi划分，而非传统SAE通过学习得到的潜在维度。该方法无需预设字典大小，利用激活空间的几何结构自动生成特征区域。

Result: EP方法在Gemma-2-2B模型上表现出色：构建计算量比SAE降低了约1000倍；在AxBench概念检测任务中AUROC达到0.881，性能接近SAE；其区域具有明确的可解释性，支持通过干预示例来控制模型行为（如拒绝回答）；并能有效分离微调前后的特征演变。此外，EP距离还能直接用于推断时的分布外（OOD）检测。

Conclusion: Exemplar Partitioning（EP）证明了基于Voronoi划分的无监督特征提取方法在计算效率上具有显著优势，且能够提供具备高度可解释性和因果干预能力的字典。这种方法为模型可解释性研究提供了一种轻量级、跨模型且具备一致性的分析工具，在保持高准确率的同时大幅降低了构建成本。

Abstract: We introduce Exemplar Partitioning (EP), an unsupervised method for constructing interpretable feature dictionaries from large language model activations with $\sim 10^{3}\times$ fewer tokens than comparable sparse autoencoders (SAEs). An EP dictionary is a Voronoi partition of activation space, built by leader-clustering streamed activations within a distance threshold. Each region is anchored by an observed exemplar that serves as both its membership criterion and intervention direction; dictionary size is not prespecified, but determined by the activation geometry at that threshold. Because exemplars are observed rather than learned, dictionaries built from the same data stream are directly comparable across layers, models, and training checkpoints.
  We characterise EP as an interpretability object via targeted demonstrations of properties newly accessible through this construction, plus one head-to-head benchmark. In Gemma-2-2B, EP dictionary regions are interpretable and support causal interventions: refusal in instruction-tuned Gemma concentrates in a region whose exemplar ablation can collapse held-out refusal. Cross-checkpoint matching between base and instruction-tuned dictionaries separates the directions preserved through finetuning from those introduced by it. EP regions and Gemma Scope SAE features decompose activation space differently but agree on a shared core: $\sim 20\%$ of EP regions match an SAE feature at $F_{1} > 0.5$, and EP one-hot probes retain $\sim 97\%$ of raw-activation probe accuracy at $\ell_{0} = 1$. Nearest-exemplar distance provides a free out-of-distribution signal at inference. On AxBench latent concept detection at Gemma-2-2B-it L20, EP at $p_{1}$ reaches mean AUROC $0.881$, $+0.126$ over the canonical GemmaScope SAE leaderboard entry and within $0.030$ of SAE-A's $0.911$, at $\sim 10^{3}\times$ less build compute.

</details>


### [171] [RQ-MoE: Residual Quantization via Mixture of Experts for Efficient Input-Dependent Vector Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14359)
*Zhengjia Zhong,Shuyan Ke,Zaizhou Lin,Jiaqi Song,Hongyi Lan,Hui Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RQ-MoE 提出了一种基于混合专家模型的动态量化框架，通过解耦量化过程，在提升高维嵌入压缩表达能力的同时，解决了传统残差量化解码慢的问题，实现了高精度与高并行效率的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的向量量化方法（如固定码本的残差量化）在处理异构数据时表达能力受限，而现有的动态量化方法（如QINCo）虽然改善了表达能力，但由于存在严格的序列依赖关系，导致解码速度缓慢，形成了计算瓶颈。因此，需要一种既能保持输入自适应性又能实现并行高效解码的量化框架。

Method: 提出了“残差量化专家混合模型”（RQ-MoE），引入了两级MoE架构与双流量化机制。该方法通过输入依赖的动态码本构建，将指令（即专家选择）与量化过程解耦，从而打破了传统残差量化的序列依赖，实现了高效的并行解码。此外，研究还通过理论分析推导了专家维度的设置准则。

Result: 实验结果表明，RQ-MoE 在重构精度和检索任务上达到了或优于现有的最先进水平（SOTA），同时在解码速度上比传统的向量量化方法快 6 倍至 14 倍。理论上也证明了标准残差量化和 QINCo 是 RQ-MoE 的特例。

Conclusion: RQ-MoE 证明了在向量量化中引入专家混合模型（MoE）是解决静态码本局限性与顺序解码瓶颈的有效途径。通过解耦指令与量化，该框架在保持高质量重构与检索性能的同时，实现了显著的并行化加速，为高维嵌入压缩提供了新的高效范式。

Abstract: Vector quantization is a fundamental tool for compressing high-dimensional embeddings, yet existing multi-codebook methods rely on static codebooks that limit expressiveness under heterogeneous data geometry. While recent dynamic quantizers like QINCo adapt codebooks to individual inputs and improve expressiveness, their strict sequential dependencies create decoding bottlenecks. We propose Residual Quantization via Mixture of Experts (RQ-MoE), a framework combining a two-level MoE with dual-stream quantization to enable input-dependent codebook adaptation for efficient vector quantization. RQ-MoE enables dynamic codebook construction and decouples instruction from quantization, facilitating parallel decoding. Theoretically, we show that standard Residual Quantization and QINCo can be recovered as constrained special cases of RQ-MoE, and derive a guideline for setting expert dimensionality in RQ-MoE. Extensive experiments show that RQ-MoE achieves state-of-the-art or on-par performance in reconstruction and retrieval, while providing 6x-14x faster decoding than prior vector quantization methods. The implementation is available at https://github.com/KDEGroup/RQ-MoE.

### [172] [MoRe: Modular Representations for Principled Continual Representation Learning on Squantial Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14364)
*Jiaqi Sun,Boyang Sun,Mohamad Rasmy,Xiangchen Song,Kun Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了MoRe框架，通过在表征层面构建层级化的模块化结构，利用数据的时间依赖性实现知识的高效解构与复用，从而在保持旧知识的同时实现持续学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续学习方法多依赖于任务特定的参数或架构修改，忽略了表征本身的结构化需求。作者旨在解决如何在不干扰已有表示的前提下，通过挖掘数据内在的组织规律，实现对新信息的原则性适应，从而平衡模型的塑性与稳定性。

Method: 作者提出了MoRe框架，其核心思想是在表征空间内识别模块化结构，而非在架构层面进行硬性切分。通过将知识解构为基础模块和特定模块的层级结构，MoRe利用序列数据的时延依赖性作为自然信号，在持续学习过程中实现模块的选择性更新、对齐与扩展。

Result: 在合成基准测试和真实大语言模型（LLM）激活数据集上的实验表明，MoRe能够识别出可解释的层级结构，显著优化了塑性与稳定性之间的权衡，并证明了其在持续适应场景下的有效性。

Conclusion: MoRe框架通过在表征层面引入层级化模块化结构，成功解决了持续学习中灾难性遗忘与知识获取的矛盾。研究表明，利用序列数据的时延依赖性来解构知识，能有效提升模型的塑性与稳定性，并为持续适应提供了一个具有可解释性的理论基础。

Abstract: Continual learning requires models to adapt to new data while preserving previously acquired knowledge. At its core, this challenge can be viewed as principled one-step adaptation: incorporating new information with minimal interference to existing representations. Most existing approaches address this challenge by modifying model parameters or architectures in a supervised, task-specific manner. However, the underlying issue is representational: tasks require distinct yet structured representations that can be selectively updated without disrupting representations, while structure should reflect intrinsic organization in the data rather than task boundaries. In sequential data, time-delayed dependencies provide a natural signal for uncovering this organization, revealing how fundamental representations give rise to more specific ones. Inspired by the modular organization of the human brain, we propose MoRe, a framework that identifies modularity in the representation itself rather than allocating it at the architectural level. MoRe decomposes knowledge into a hierarchy of fundamental and specific modules with identifiability guarantees, enabling principled module reuse, alignment, and expansion during adaptation while preserving old modules by construction. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks and real-world LLM activations demonstrate interpretable hierarchical structure, improved plasticity-stability trade-offs, suggesting MoRe as a principled foundation for continual adaptation

</details>


### [173] [LoMETab: Beyond Rank-1 Ensembles for Tabular Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14365)
*Changryeol Choi,Hyewon Park,Yujin Kwon,Gowun Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 LoMETab，这是一种通过低秩分解对乘法隐式集成模型进行泛化的新方法。该方法引入了可调节的秩和初始化参数，通过增强模型成员间的预测多样性，实现了对隐式集成模型行为的有效控制与优化，从而在表格数据学习中表现出比固定结构更强的灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表格学习领域的基准测试显示，领先模型（包括梯度提升树、注意力架构和隐式集成模型）的性能表现日益趋同，难以产生显著的性能跃升。因此，研究的重点转向理解并控制那些使简单的神经表格模型具有竞争力的潜在机制，以实现更优的集成效果和多样性控制。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为 LoMETab 的模型，该模型是对乘法隐式集成（如 BatchEnsemble/TabM）的秩 $r$ 泛化。它通过将权重参数化为 $W_k = W \odot (1 + A_kB_k^\top)$，其中 $W$ 为共享权重，$A_k$ 和 $B_k$ 为成员特定的低秩因子。该方法引入了两个核心多样性控制轴：适配器秩 $r$ 和初始化尺度 $\sigma_{\mathrm{init}}$。作者通过理论证明了 $r \ge 2$ 时该方法严格扩展了 BatchEnsemble 的假设空间。

Result: 实验结果表明，LoMETab 能够产生可度量的预测多样性。在代表性分类数据集上，LoMETab 的成员间 KL 散度优于加性低秩消融方法，且通过调整 $r$ 和 $\sigma_{\mathrm{init}}$ 可以实现对多样性的跨数量级控制。这种多样性体现在决策层面（如 argmax 不一致性）和输出层面（如回归任务的歧义性）。此外，性能表现随数据不同而展现出对 $(r, \sigma_{\mathrm{init}})$ 网格的不同依赖性。

Conclusion: LoMETab 证明了通过引入低秩自适应（Low-rank adaptation）机制，可以有效地扩展隐式集成模型（如 TabM）的假设空间。研究结果表明，通过调节适配器秩（rank $r$）和初始化尺度（$\sigma_{\mathrm{init}}$），可以实现对模型成员预测多样性的精确控制，从而为表格数据学习提供了一种灵活且可配置的集成框架，而非仅仅局限于固定的秩 1 模型。

Abstract: Recent tabular learning benchmarks increasingly show a tight performance cluster rather than a clear hierarchy among leading methods, spanning gradient boosted decision trees, attention-based architectures, and implicit ensembles such as TabM. As benchmark gains plateau, a complementary goal is to understand and control the mechanisms that make simple neural tabular models competitive. We propose LoMETab, a rank-$r$ generalization of multiplicative implicit ensembles. LoMETab lifts the rank-1 BatchEnsemble/TabM modulation to a rank-$r$ identity-residual Hadamard family by parameterizing each member weight as $W_k = W \odot (1 + A_kB_k^\top)$, where $W$ is shared and $(A_k, B_k)$ are member-specific low-rank factors. This exposes two practical diversity-control axes: the adapter rank $r$ and the initialization scale $σ_{\mathrm{init}}$, and we prove that for $r \ge 2$ this generalization strictly enlarges BatchEnsemble's hypothesis class. Empirically, we show that this added capacity manifests as measurable predictive diversity after training: on representative classification datasets, LoMETab sustains higher pairwise KL than an additive low-rank ablation, and $(r, σ_{\mathrm{init}})$ provides broad control over pairwise KL, varying by up to several orders of magnitude across configurations. The induced diversity is reflected in task-appropriate output-level measures: argmax disagreement for classification and ambiguity for regression, indicating that the control extends beyond pairwise KL to decision- and output-level member variation. Finally, experiments sweeping over adapter rank $r$ and initialization scale $σ_{\mathrm{init}}$ reveal that predictive performance is dataset-dependent over the $(r, σ_{\mathrm{init}})$ grid, supporting LoMETab as a controllable family of implicit ensembles rather than a fixed rank-1 construction.

</details>


### [174] [Turning Stale Gradients into Stable Gradients: Coherent Coordinate Descent with Implicit Landscape Smoothing for Lightweight Zeroth-Order Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14373)
*Chen Liang,Xiatao Sun,Qian Wang,Daniel Rakita*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 CoCD 的确定性零阶优化算法，通过巧妙利用历史梯度信息，在保持 O(1) 查询复杂度的同时，克服了传统零阶优化方法在样本效率和稳定性方面的权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的零阶（ZO）优化方法在样本效率和梯度估计方差之间面临严重的权衡：传统的有限差分方法样本效率低下，而基于随机空间的估计方法则存在高方差问题。研究旨在设计一种既具备样本效率又具备预算意识的确定性零阶优化器。

Method: 提出了“连贯坐标下降”（Coherent Coordinate Descent, CoCD）算法。该方法将零阶优化问题转化为带“热启动”的块循环坐标下降（BCCD），利用历史（陈旧）梯度信息作为计算资产，从而实现每步 O(1) 的查询复杂度，并保持全局下降方向。此外，研究还揭示了增大有限差分步长可通过隐含的平滑效应提升收敛稳定性。

Result: 实验证明，CoCD 在 MLP、CNN 和 ResNet 等模型（高达 27 万参数）上，相较于传统的 BCCD，在样本效率和收敛精度上表现出显著优势，并展现出比随机化零阶优化方法更优的稳定性。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，确定性且具有结构意识的更新机制，在轻量级零阶优化场景中表现优于随机化方法。通过有效利用历史梯度信息，CoCD 能够以极低的查询复杂度实现更稳定、更高效的优化。

Abstract: Zeroth-Order (ZO) optimization is pivotal for scenarios where backpropagation is unavailable, such as memory-constrained on-device learning and black-box optimization. However, existing methods face a stark trade-off: they are either sample-inefficient (e.g., standard finite differences) or suffer from high variance due to randomized estimation (e.g., random subspace methods). In this work, we propose Coherent Coordinate Descent (CoCD), a deterministic, sample-efficient, and budget-aware ZO optimizer. Theoretically, we formalize the notion of gradient coherence and demonstrate that CoCD is equivalent to Block Cyclic Coordinate Descent (BCCD) with ``warm starts,'' effectively converting historical (stale) gradients from a liability into a computational asset. This mechanism enables $O(1)$ query complexity per step while maintaining global descent directions. Furthermore, we derive error bounds revealing a counter-intuitive insight: larger finite-difference step sizes can induce an implicit smoothing effect on the optimization landscape by reducing the effective smoothness constant, thereby improving convergence stability. Experiments on MLP, CNN, and ResNet architectures (up to 270k parameters) demonstrate that CoCD significantly outperforms BCCD in terms of sample efficiency and convergence loss/accuracy, and exhibits superior stability over randomized ZO methods. Our results suggest that deterministic, structure-aware updates offer a superior alternative to randomization for lightweight ZO optimization.

</details>

Method: 提出了一种基于混合整数规划（MIP）的最优模式检测树（OPDT）模型，用于在二分类任务中发现单一最优规则；同时引入了分支结构约束（BSC）框架，允许决策者将领域知识和业务约束直接集成到模型优化过程中。

Result: 计算实验表明，OPDT能够在合理的时间内在中等规模数据集上发现具有最优性保证的模式，并在满足业务约束的同时有效平衡覆盖率与误报率。

Conclusion: OPDT是一种能够提供最优性保证的解释性规则挖掘方法，通过引入分支结构约束（BSC），它能够有效地结合领域知识，在医疗、风险评估等对可解释性要求高的领域具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Pattern discovery in data plays a crucial role across diverse domains, including healthcare, risk assessment, and machinery maintenance. In contrast to black-box deep learning models, symbolic rule discovery emerges as a key data mining task, generating human-interpretable rules that offer both transparency and intuitive explainability. This paper introduces the Optimal Pattern Detection Tree (OPDT), a rule-based machine learning model based on novel mixed-integer programming to discover a single optimal pattern in data through binary classification. To incorporate prior knowledge and compliance requirements, we further introduce the Branching Structure Constraints (BSC) framework, which enables decision makers to encode domain knowledge and constraints directly into the model. This optimization-based approach discovers a hidden underlying pattern in datasets, when it exists, by identifying an optimal rule that maximizes coverage while minimizing the false positive rate due to misclassification. Our computational experiments show that OPDT discovers a pattern with optimality guarantees on moderately sized datasets within reasonable runtime.

### [176] [Data-Augmented Game Starts for Accelerating Self-Play Exploration in Imperfect Information Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14379)
*JB Lanier,Nathan Monette,Pierre Baldi,Roy Fox*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 DAGS 的多智能体训练策略，通过从人类专家数据中采样中间状态来加速非完美信息博弈中的强化学习探索，有效解决了长期任务中探索困难的问题，并确保了均衡的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模非完美信息竞争博弈（如星际争霸、Dota等）中，由于奖励稀疏和长程探索困难，寻找近似均衡在计算上不可行。现有的在线探索方法难以有效覆盖复杂的战略空间，因此需要一种能更高效利用离线数据以指导探索的方法。

Method: 提出了“数据增强游戏启动”（Data-Augmented Game Starts, DAGS）方法。该方法从人类专家演示数据中采样中间状态作为强化学习的起始点，以引导智能体快速进入具有战略意义的子博弈进行探索，并采用多任务观察标记（multi-task observation flags）来纠正因起始状态分布变化而引入的均衡偏差。

Result: 在 Kuhn Poker、Goofspiel 等实验中，DAGS 在固定计算预算下实现了更低的不可利用性（exploitability），证明了其在解决高难度探索博弈方面的有效性。此外，作者还发布了一套新的基准环境，用以测试模型处理大规模状态空间的能力。

Conclusion: DAGS 是一种高效的训练策略，通过利用离线专家数据初始化多智能体强化学习的起始状态，显著改善了长程、大规模非完美信息博弈中的探索效率。通过引入多任务观察标记（multi-task observation flags），有效解决了起始状态分布变化带来的均衡偏移问题。该研究为解决复杂博弈环境下的训练瓶颈提供了可扩展的方案。

Abstract: Finding approximate equilibria for large-scale imperfect-information competitive games such as StarCraft, Dota, and CounterStrike remains computationally infeasible due to sparse rewards and challenging exploration over long horizons. In this paper, we propose a multi-agent starting-state sampling strategy designed to substantially accelerate online exploration in regularized policy-gradient game methods for two-player zero-sum (2p0s) games. Motivated by an assumption that offline demonstrations from skilled humans can provide good coverage of high-level strategies relevant to equilibrium play, we propose the initialization of reinforcement learning data collection at intermediate states sampled from offline data to facilitate exploration of strategically relevant subgames. Referring to this method as Data-Augmented Game Starts (DAGS), we perform experiments using synthetic datasets and analytically tractable, long-horizon control variants of two-player Kuhn Poker, Goofspiel, and a counterexample game designed to penalize biased beliefs over hidden information. Under fixed computational budgets, DAGS enables regularized policy gradient methods to achieve lower exploitability in games with significantly more challenging exploration. We show that augmenting starting state distributions when solving imperfect information games can lead to biased equilibria, and we provide a straightforward mitigation to this in the form of multi-task observation flags. Finally, we release a new set of benchmark environments that drastically increase exploration challenges and state counts in existing OpenSpiel games while keeping exploitability measurements analytically tractable.

Method: 研究提出了 NodeSynth 方法，该方法使用一种基于真实世界证据微调的分类学生成器（TaG）来构建具有社会相关性的合成查询，并通过对多种主流大模型进行压力测试与消融实验来验证其有效性。

Abstract: Recent advancements in generative AI facilitate large-scale synthetic data generation for model evaluation. However, without targeted approaches, these datasets often lack the sociotechnical nuance required for sensitive domains. We introduce NodeSynth, an evidence-grounded methodology that generates socially relevant synthetic queries by leveraging a fine-tuned taxonomy generator (TaG) anchored in real-world evidence. Evaluated against four mainstream LLMs (e.g., Claude 4.5 Haiku), NodeSynth elicited failure rates up to five times higher than human-authored benchmarks. Ablation studies confirm that our granular taxonomic expansion significantly drives these failure rates, while independent validation reveals critical deficiencies in prominent guard models (e.g., Llama-Guard-3). We open-source our end-to-end research prototype and datasets to enable scalable, high-stakes model evaluation and targeted safety interventions (https://github.com/google-research/nodesynth).

Empirically, GeoViSTA's unified embeddings improve linear probing performance on high-impact downstream tasks, outperforming baselines in predicting disease-specific mortality and fire hazard frequency across held-out regions. These results demonstrate that jointly modeling the physical environment alongside structured socioeconomic context yields highly transferable representations for holistic geospatial inference.

### [179] [What if Tomorrow is the World Cup Final? Counterfactual Time Series Forecasting with Textual Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14422)

In this context, forecasting must dynamically adapt to complex and stochastic future conditions, which introduces fundamental challenges in both forecasting and evaluation. Traditional methods typically rely on historical data or factual future conditions, while overlooking counterfactual scenarios. Furthermore, many existing approaches are restricted to simple structured conditions, limiting their ability to generalize to the real-world complexities. To address these gaps, we introduce the task of counterfactual time series forecasting with textual conditions, enabling more flexible and condition-aware forecasting. We propose a comprehensive evaluation framework that encompasses both factual and counterfactual settings, even in the absence of ground truth time series. Additionally, we present a novel text-attribution mechanism that distinguishes mutable from immutable factors, thereby improving forecast accuracy under sophisticated and stochastic textual conditions. The project page is at https://seqml.github.io/TADiff/

</details>


### [180] [Collaborative Yet Personalized Policy Training: Single-Timescale Federated Actor-Critic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14423)
*Leo Muxing Wang,Pengkun Yang,Lili Su*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种联邦演员-评论家框架，通过共享线性子空间实现了个性化与协作的平衡。该方法不仅在理论上证明了在异构马尔可夫环境下的有限时间收敛性和针对智能体数量的线性加速，还在实际实验中验证了其优越的训练表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的演员-评论家方法在多智能体协作中要么忽视环境异构性，要么直接训练单一共享策略而牺牲个性化，导致在处理具有差异化状态转移概率的联邦场景时表现不佳。因此，研究旨在开发一种能够在利用联邦学习实现知识共享的同时，保持智能体个性化策略的框架。

Method: 提出了一种联邦演员-评论家框架，通过学习共享的线性子空间表示来兼顾公共知识与个体差异。该方法采用单时间尺度更新策略，结合联合线性近似框架，并利用扰动分析（针对子空间更新与QR分解）和条件混合论证（处理异构马尔可夫噪声），实现了对局部策略和评论家的迭代优化。此外，还通过细粒度分析量化了马尔可夫采样与固定策略采样之间的差异。

Result: 理论上证明了该框架的有限时间收敛性：评论家误差收敛速度为 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/((1-γ)^4\sqrt{TK}))$，策略梯度范数收敛速度为 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/((1-γ)^6\sqrt{TK}))$，实现了相对于智能体数量 $K$ 的线性加速。实验结果表明，该方法在 `Hopper-v5` 等异构任务中优于传统的单体 PPO 和联邦平均 PPO 方法，并展现了良好的知识迁移性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的联邦演员-评论家（Federated Actor-Critic）框架通过共享线性子空间表示实现了个性化策略学习，在异构环境下有效提升了训练效率，并具备理论上的收敛保障和线性加速特性，为联邦强化学习在异构场景中的应用提供了坚实的理论与实践支持。

Abstract: Despite the popularity of the actor-critic method and the practical needs of collaborative policy training, existing works typically either overlook environmental heterogeneity or give up personalization altogether by training a single shared policy across all agents. We consider a federated actor-critic framework in which agents share a common linear subspace representation while maintaining personalized local policy components, and agents iteratively estimate the common subspace, local critic heads, and local policies (i.e., actors). Under canonical single-timescale updates with Markovian sampling, we establish finite-time convergence via a novel joint linear approximation framework. Specifically, we show that the critic error converges to zero at the rate of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/((1-γ)^4\sqrt{TK}))$, and the policy gradient norm converges to zero at the rate of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/((1-γ)^6\sqrt{TK}))$, where $T$ is the number of rounds, $K$ is the number of agents, and $γ\in (0,1)$ is the discount factor. These results demonstrate linear speedup with respect to the number of agents $K$, despite heterogeneous Markovian trajectories under distinct transition kernels and coupled learning dynamics. To address these challenges, we develop a new perturbation analysis for the projected subspace updates and QR decomposition steps, together with conditional mixing arguments for heterogeneous Markovian noise. Furthermore, to handle the additional complications induced by policy updates and temporal dependence, we establish fine-grained characterizations of the discrepancies between function evaluations under Markovian sampling and under temporally frozen policies. Experiments instantiate the framework within PPO on federated \texttt{Hopper-v5} action-map heterogeneity, showing gains over Single PPO and FedAvg PPO and downstream transfer from the learned shared trunk.

### [181] [FrontierSmith: Synthesizing Open-Ended Coding Problems at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14445)
*Runyuan He,Qiuyang Mang,Shang Zhou,Kaiyuan Liu,Hanchen Li,Huanzhi Mao,Qizheng Zhang,Zerui Li,Bo Peng,Lufeng Cheng,Tianfu Fu,Yichuan Wang,Wenhao Chai,Jingbo Shang,Alex Dimakis,Joseph E. Gonzalez,Alvin Cheung*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了FrontierSmith自动化系统。该系统以现有的封闭式竞赛编程题为种子，通过修改目标、限制输出和泛化输入来迭代演化生成开放式任务候选集；利用“想法发散度指标（Idea Divergence Metric）”筛选出能够引发多样化解决方案的问题，并由智能体自动生成相应的测试用例和验证器。

Conclusion: 通过使用FrontierSmith自动生成的开放式编码数据进行训练，可以显著提升大语言模型在开放式编程任务中的性能。这证明了从封闭式任务演进生成高质量开放式数据是提升模型长周期编程能力的有效路径。

Abstract: Many real-world coding challenges are open-ended and admit no known optimal solution. Yet, recent progress in LLM coding has focused on well-defined tasks such as feature implementation, bug fixing, and competitive programming. Open-ended coding remains a weak spot for LLMs, largely because open-ended training problems are scarce and expensive to construct. Our goal is to synthesize open-ended coding problems at scale to train stronger LLM coders. We introduce FrontierSmith, an automated system for iteratively evolving open-ended problems from existing closed-ended coding tasks. Starting from competitive programming problems, FrontierSmith generates candidate open-ended variants by changing the problems'goals, restricting outputs, and generalizing inputs. It then uses a quantitative idea divergence metric to select problems that elicit genuinely diverse approaches from different solvers. Agents then generate test cases and verifiers for the surviving candidates. On two open-ended coding benchmarks, training on our synthesized data yields substantial gains over the base models: Qwen3.5-9B improves by +8.82 score on FrontierCS and +306.36 (Elo-rating-based performance) on ALE-bench; Qwen3.5-27B improves by +12.12 and +309.12, respectively. The synthesized problems also make agents take more turns and use more tokens, similar to human-curated ones, suggesting that closed-ended seeds can be a practical starting point for long-horizon coding data.

### [182] [When Answers Stray from Questions: Hallucination Detection via Question-Answer Orthogonal Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14449)
*Siyang Yao,Erhu Feng,Yubin Xia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 QAOD 的高效幻觉检测框架，通过从答案表示中剥离问题相关分量，成功克服了传统白盒探测在领域偏移下性能下降的问题，在极低计算成本下实现了行业领先的跨领域泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测方法存在局限性：黑盒一致性方法推理成本过高；单次白盒探测方法虽然高效，但往往孤立处理答案表示，在面对分布偏移（Domain Shift）时性能会显著下降。因此，需要一种既能保持高效，又能兼顾准确性与跨领域稳健性的检测手段。

Method: 提出 QAOD（问题-答案正交分解）框架。该方法首先从答案表示中正交投影出与问题相关的方向，以去除领域条件的噪声；接着通过“多样性惩罚的 Fisher 评分”选择关键层，并利用 Fisher 重要性筛选判别性神经元；最后设计了联合探测（结合问题上下文提升领域内性能）和正交探测（仅保留正交分量以实现稳健的领域外迁移）两种互补策略。

Result: QAOD 的联合探测策略在所有评估模型中实现了最佳的领域内 AUROC；其仅使用正交分量的探测策略在领域外（OOD）迁移表现上最为突出，在 BioASQ 数据集上性能超越最佳白盒基准 21%，且推理成本不到基准方案的 25%。

Conclusion: QAOD 通过正交分解技术实现了在保持低计算成本的同时，显著提升了 LLM 幻觉检测在领域内和跨领域场景下的准确性与泛化能力。该方法证明了将答案表示与问题上下文解耦，是提取与领域无关的忠实度信号的关键。

Abstract: Hallucination detection in large language models (LLMs) requires balancing accu racy, efficiency, and robustness to distribution shift. Black-box consistency methods are effective but demand repeated inference; single-pass white-box probes are effi cient yet treat answer representations in isolation, often degrading sharply under domain shift. We propose QAOD (Question-Answer Orthogonal Decomposition), a single-pass framework that projects away the question-aligned direction from the answer representation to obtain a question-orthogonal component that suppresses domain-conditioned variation. To identify informative signals, QAOD further selects layers via diversity-penalized Fisher scoring and discriminative neurons via Fisher importance. To address both in-domain detection and cross-domain generalization, we design two complementary probing strategies: pairing the or thogonal component with question context yields a joint probe that maximizes in-domain discriminability, while using the orthogonal component alone preserves domain-agnostic factuality signals for robust transfer. QAOD's joint probe achieves the best in-domain AUROC across all evaluated model-dataset pairs, while the orthogonal-only probe delivers the strongest OOD transfer, surpassing the best white-box baseline by up to 21% on BioASQ at under 25% of generation cost.

</details>


### [183] [LiSA: Lifelong Safety Adaptation via Conservative Policy Induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14454)
*Minbeom Kim,Lesly Miculicich,Bhavana Dalvi Mishra,Mihir Parmar,Phillip Wallis,Bharath Chandrasekhar,Kyomin Jung,Tomas Pfister,Long T. Le*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LiSA 是一种用于 AI 智能体的终身安全适应框架，通过结构化记忆将稀疏的反馈转化为可复用的安全规则，有效提升了系统在复杂、动态环境下的安全防护能力与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 AI 智能体功能复杂化，传统的预部署防护机制难以应对动态、上下文依赖性强的安全挑战。现有的反馈机制通常稀疏且存在噪声，频繁的微调在实际工程中不可行，导致安全防护与动态部署环境之间存在脱节。

Method: LiSA（终身安全适应）框架：1. 策略抽象：将偶尔的失败转化为可复用的抽象规则；2. 冲突感知局部规则：通过引入局部规则防止在混合标签场景下的过度泛化；3. 证据感知置信度门控：基于后验下界机制，使得记忆复用随着证据积累而扩展，而非仅仅依赖经验准确率。

Result: 在 PrivacyLens+、ConFaide+ 和 AgentHarm 等基准测试中，LiSA 在稀疏反馈环境下显著优于现有的记忆基准模型，即使在高达 20% 的标签噪声（标签翻转）下仍保持稳健，并显著提升了延迟-性能表现。

Conclusion: LiSA 为确保 AI 智能体在面对复杂且不断变化的现实环境时能够安全运行提供了一种高效、可扩展的解决方案，能够有效应对由于上下文环境多变而导致的安全防护“最后一公里”问题。

Abstract: As AI agents move from chat interfaces to systems that read private data, call tools, and execute multi-step workflows, guardrails become a last line of defense against concrete deployment harms. In these settings, guardrail failures are no longer merely answer-quality errors: they can leak secrets, authorize unsafe actions, or block legitimate work. The hardest failures are often contextual: whether an action is acceptable depends on local privacy norms, organizational policies, and user expectations that resist pre-deployment specification. This creates a practical gap: guardrails must adapt to their own operating environments, yet deployment feedback is typically limited to sparse, noisy user-reported failures, and repeated fine-tuning is often impractical. To address this gap, we propose LiSA (Lifelong Safety Adaptation), a conservative policy induction framework that improves a fixed base guardrail through structured memory. LiSA converts occasional failures into reusable policy abstractions so that sparse reports can generalize beyond individual cases, adds conflict-aware local rules to prevent overgeneralization in mixed-label contexts, and applies evidence-aware confidence gating via a posterior lower bound, so that memory reuse scales with accumulated evidence rather than empirical accuracy alone. Across PrivacyLens+, ConFaide+, and AgentHarm, LiSA consistently outperforms strong memory-based baselines under sparse feedback, remains robust under noisy user feedback even at 20% label-flip rates, and pushes the latency--performance frontier beyond backbone model scaling. Ultimately, LiSA offers a practical path to secure AI agents against the unpredictable long tail of real-world edge risks.

Abstract: We propose a new method of learning from positive and unlabeled (PU) examples in highly imbalanced datasets. Often, training data comprises positive and unlabeled instances, the latter typically being dominated by negative, but including also several positive instances. While PU learning is well-studied, few methods address imbalanced settings or hard-to-detect positive examples that resemble negative ones. Our approach uses a focused empirical risk estimator, incorporating both positive and unlabeled examples to train binary classifiers. Method: 提出了一种基于舒尔分解（Schur decomposition）的投影方案，通过将状态矩阵的准三角因子动态投影到其最近的稳定空间，并开发了预因式分解公式以确保线性离散时间状态空间层的渐近稳定性。

Abstract: Building black-box models for dynamical systems from data is a challenging problem in machine learning, especially when asymptotic stability guarantees are required. In this paper, we introduce a novel stability-ensuring and backpropagation-compatible projection scheme based on the Schur decomposition for the state matrix of linear discrete-time state-space layers, as well as an alternative pre-factorized formulation of the methodology. The proposed methods dynamically project the quasi-triangular factor of the state matrix's real Schur decomposition onto its nearest stable peer, ensuring stable dynamics with minimal overparameterization. Experiments on synthetic linear systems demonstrate that the method achieves accuracy and convergence rates comparable to those of state-of-the-art stable-system identification techniques, despite a marginal increase in computational complexity. Furthermore, the lower weight count facilitates convergence during training without sacrificing accuracy in stacked neural-network architectures with static nonlinearities targeting real-world datasets. These results suggest that the Schur-based projection provides a numerically robust framework for identifying complex dynamics on par with the State of the Art while satisfying strict asymptotic-stability requirements.

### [187] [Lang2MLIP: End-to-End Language-to-Machine Learning Interatomic Potential Development with Autonomous Agentic Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14527)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为Lang2MLIP的多智能体框架，将MLIP的开发过程建模为由大语言模型（LLM）驱动的序列决策问题。该框架取消了固定的流水线设计，智能体通过观察数据集、模型状态、评估结果及日志，动态决定改进模型的后续操作，并具备自我纠错和重新规划的能力。

Result: 通过在具有多种组件和界面的固体电解质界面（SEI）系统上的实验验证，表明Lang2MLIP能够成功实现端到端的MLIP开发，证明了该方法在自动化材料建模方面的潜力和有效性。

Conclusion: 基于大语言模型的多智能体框架Lang2MLIP是实现机器学习原子间势（MLIP）开发自动化的有效途径，能够显著降低非专家的使用门槛，并为处理复杂材料体系提供了一种灵活、自适应的解决方案。

Abstract: Developing machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) for complex materials systems remains challenging because it requires expertise in atomistic simulations, machine learning, and workflow design, as well as iterative active learning procedures. Existing automated pipelines typically assume a fixed sequence of stages or depend on domain experts, which limits their adaptability to heterogeneous materials systems where the optimal curriculum is not known in advance. To lower the barrier to developing MLIPs for non-experts, we propose Lang2MLIP, a multi-agent framework that takes natural-language input and formulates end-to-end MLIP development as a sequential decision-making problem solved by large language models (LLMs). At each step, a decision-making agent observes the current dataset, model, evaluation results, and execution log, and then automatically selects an appropriate action to improve the model. This removes the need for a predefined pipeline and enables the agent to self-correct by revisiting earlier subsystems when new failures arise. We evaluate this approach on a solid electrolyte interphase (SEI) system with multiple components and interfaces. These results suggest that LLM-based multi-agent systems are a promising direction for automating MLIP development and making it more accessible to non-experts.

</details>


### [188] [Resolving Action Bottleneck: Agentic Reinforcement Learning Informed by Token-Level Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14558)
*Langzhou He,Junyou Zhu,Yue Zhou,Zhengyao Gu,Junhua Liu,Wei-Chieh Huang,Henry Peng Zou,David Wipf,Philip S. Yu,Qitian Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型智能体强化学习中训练信号分配不均的问题，该论文提出了ActFocus方法，通过对推理令牌降权并强化行动令牌的训练权重，显著提升了模型在多步推理任务中的性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体强化学习（如PPO、GRPO）对多轮轨迹中的所有令牌采取统一的梯度更新策略，忽视了推理令牌与行动令牌在任务贡献度上的本质差异，导致训练信号分配不均。作者发现存在“行动瓶颈（Action Bottleneck）”现象，即奖励信号主要集中在行动令牌上，而推理令牌在训练中被过度强化。

Method: 作者提出了ActFocus方法，核心在于令牌重加权（token reweighting）。该方法首先通过对推理过程中的推理令牌（reasoning tokens）进行梯度降权，减少其对模型更新的干扰；其次，引入基于能量模型的重分配机制，根据行动令牌（action tokens）的不确定性动态增加其权重，从而实现更精准的学分分配（credit assignment）。

Result: 在四个不同任务环境中进行评估，ActFocus在模型大小各异的情况下，均显著优于基准方法PPO和GRPO。在最终步骤的表现上，相比PPO和GRPO分别提升了高达65.2和63.7个百分点，且在运行时和显存使用方面没有增加任何额外成本。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的ActFocus策略通过优化奖励分配机制，成功解决了智能体强化学习中的“行动瓶颈”问题。实验证明，对推理令牌进行梯度降权并强化行动令牌的权重，能够显著提升大语言模型在多步推理任务中的性能，且无需额外的计算开销，为高效的智能体训练提供了新路径。

Abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning trains large language models using multi-turn trajectories that interleave long reasoning traces with short environment-facing actions. Common policy-gradient methods, such as PPO and GRPO, treat each token in a trajectory equally, leading to uniform credit assignment. In this paper, we critically demonstrate that such uniform credit assignment largely misallocates token-level training signals. From an energy-based modeling perspective, we show that token-level training signals, quantified by their correlations with reward variance of different rollouts sampled from a given prompt, concentrate sharply on action tokens rather than reasoning tokens, even though action tokens account for only a small fraction of the trajectory. We refer to this phenomenon as the Action Bottleneck. Motivated by this observation, we propose an embarrassingly simple token reweighting approach, ActFocus, that downweights gradients on reasoning tokens, along with an additional energy-based redistribution mechanism that further increases the weights on action tokens with higher uncertainty. Across four environments and different model sizes, ActFocus consistently outperforms PPO and GRPO, yielding final-step gains of up to 65.2 and 63.7 percentage points, respectively, without any additional runtime or memory cost.

Conclusion: RxEval 揭示了现有大语言模型在临床处方任务中仍存在显著局限，特别是在处理动态临床轨迹和精细化药物建议（剂量、途径）方面。该基准测试表明，提升模型对患者信息的理解及临床推理能力是未来医疗人工智能发展的关键。

Existing benchmarks formulate this task as admission-level prediction over coarse drug codes with multi-hot diagnostic and procedure code inputs, failing to capture the per-timepoint, information-rich nature of real prescribing. RxEval comprises 1,547 questions spanning 584 patients, 18 diagnostic categories, and 969 unique medications. Evaluation of 16 LLMs shows that RxEval is both challenging and discriminative: F1 ranges from 45.18 to 77.10 across models, and the best Exact Match is only 46.10%. Error analysis reveals that even frontier models may overlook stated patient information and fail to derive clinical conclusions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Artificial intelligence in high-stakes tabular domains cannot be evaluated by predictive performance alone, yet current practice still assesses explainability, fairness, robustness, privacy, and sustainability mostly in isolation. We propose the Model Integrity and Responsibility Assessment Index (MIRAI), a unified evaluation framework that measures tabular models across these five dimensions under a controlled comparison setting and aggregates them into a single score. MIRAI combines established metrics through normalized and direction-aligned dimension scores, which enables direct comparison across models with different architectural and computational profiles. Experiments on healthcare, financial, and socioeconomic datasets show that higher predictive performance does not necessarily imply better overall integrity and responsibility. In several cases, simpler models achieve a stronger cross-dimensional balance than more complex deep tabular architectures. MIRAI provides a compact and practical basis for responsible model selection in regulated settings.

### [192] [SeesawNet: Towards Non-stationary Time Series Forecasting with Balanced Modeling of Common and Specific Dependencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14551)
*Hao Li,Lu Zhang,Liu Chong,Yankai Chen,Pengyang Wang,Yingjie Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SeesawNet 通过一种新型的自适应注意力机制，在处理非平稳时间序列时，能够动态平衡公共模式与实例特定特征，从而解决了传统实例归一化带来的特征过平滑问题，提升了预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然实例归一化（IN）在非平稳时间序列预测中常用于减少分布偏移，但它会掩盖对建模时间及跨通道异构性至关重要的实例特定结构信息。现有的改进方法未能有效解决如何在保留公共模式的同时，自适应地建模实例特定依赖的矛盾。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SeesawNet 的统一架构，核心组件是自适应平稳-非平稳注意力机制（ASNA）。ASNA 通过分别从归一化序列（提取公共依赖）和原始序列（提取特定依赖）中获取信息，并根据实例的非平稳程度进行动态融合，同时交替进行时间维度和通道维度的关系建模。

Result: 在多个真实世界的时间序列预测基准测试中，SeesawNet 的表现始终优于现有的前沿方法（SOTA）。

Conclusion: SeesawNet 通过动态平衡公共依赖与实例特定依赖，有效解决了非平稳时间序列预测中实例归一化（IN）导致的特征过平滑问题，为处理非平稳时间序列提供了一种更优的建模范式。

Abstract: Instance normalization (IN) is widely used in non-stationary multivariate time series forecasting to reduce distribution shifts and highlight common patterns across samples. However, IN can over-smooth instance-specific structural information that is essential for modeling temporal and cross-channel heterogeneity. While prior methods further suppress distribution discrepancies or attempt to recover temporal specific dependencies, they often ignore a central tension: how to adaptively model common and instance-specific dependency based on each instance's non-stationary structures. To address this dilemma, we propose SeesawNet, a unified architecture that dynamically balances common and instance-specific dependency modeling in both temporal and channel dimensions. At its core is Adaptive Stationary-Nonstationary Attention (ASNA), which captures common dependencies from normalized sequences and specific dependencies from raw sequences, and adaptively fuses them according to instance-level non-stationarity. Built upon ASNA, SeesawNet alternates dedicated temporal and channel relationship modeling to jointly capture long-range and cross-variable dependencies. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world benchmarks demonstrate that SeesawNet consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods.

### [193] [Boosting Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards via Randomly Selected Few-Shot Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15012)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has achieved great success in developing Large Language Models (LLMs) with chain-of-thought rollouts for many tasks such as math and coding. Nevertheless, RLVR struggles with sample efficiency on difficult problems where correct rollouts are hard to generate. Prior works propose to address this issue via demonstration-guided RLVR, i.e., to conduct Supervised FineTuning (SFT) when RL fails; however, SFT often requires a lot of data, which can be expensive to acquire. In this paper, we propose FEST, a FEw-ShoT demonstration-guided RLVR algorithm. It attains compelling results with only 128 demonstrations randomly selected from an SFT dataset. We find that three components are vital for the success: supervised signal, on-policy signal, and decaying weights on the few-shot SFT dataset to prevent overfitting from multiple-epoch training. On several benchmarks, FEST outperforms baselines with magnitudes less SFT data, even matching their performance with full dataset.

Abstract: Prompt engineering has become central to eliciting the capabilities of large language models (LLMs). At its core lies prompt selection -- efficiently identifying the most effective prompts. ### [195] [Woodelf++: A Fast and Unified Partial Dependence Plot Algorithm for Decision Tree Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14578)
*Ron Wettenstein,Alexander Nadel,Udi Boker*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Woodelf++，一种用于决策树集成模型的高效、统一的可解释性计算框架。通过算法优化，它能极快地计算 PDP、Joint-PDP 以及所有阶数的特征交互值（Any-Order-PDIVs），在性能上实现了相对于现有方法数量级的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的可解释性工具（如PDP、Joint-PDP和Any-Order-PDIV）在处理决策树集成模型时计算开销巨大，在大规模数据集上往往难以在合理时间内完成，限制了其实际应用。作者旨在通过算法优化，大幅降低这些工具的计算复杂度。

Method: 基于先前用于高效计算SHAP的Woodelf算法，通过在伪布尔函数上派生合适的度量标准，构建了一个统一框架来计算PDP、Joint-PDP和Any-Order-PDIV。同时，引入了利用模型分裂阈值的“全PDP”（Full PDP）以更精确地捕获模型行为，并提供了纯Python实现及GPU加速支持。

Result: Woodelf++ 在处理大规模数据集（40万行）时表现优异：PDP和Joint-PDP的计算速度比现有先进方法快6倍，比scikit-learn快5个数量级；在计算Any-Order-PDIVs时，性能提升巨大，将原本预估需要百万年的任务缩短至5分钟内完成。

Conclusion: Woodelf++ 通过提供一个高效的统一框架，成功解决了决策树集成模型中复杂可解释性工具（如PDP、Joint-PDP和Any-Order-PDIV）计算缓慢的瓶颈问题，显著提升了大规模数据集上的计算性能，为模型可解释性研究提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: Partial Dependence Plots (PDPs) visualize how changes in a single feature affect the average model prediction. They are widely used in practice to interpret decision tree ensembles and other machine learning models. Joint-PDPs extend this idea to pairs of features, revealing their combined effect. Partial Dependence Interaction Values (PDIVs) measure feature interactions. The Any-Order-PDIVs task computes these interactions for every feature subset across all rows of the dataset.
  We introduce Woodelf++, a unified and efficient approach for computing all these useful explainability tools on decision tree ensembles, building on Woodelf, an algorithm for efficient SHAP computation. By deriving suitable metrics over pseudo-Boolean functions, Woodelf++ can compute PDPs (exact and approximate), Joint-PDPs, and Any-Order-PDIVs in a unified framework. Our method delivers substantial complexity improvements over the state of the art, including an exponential gain for Any-Order-PDIVs. Additionally, we introduce and efficiently compute Full PDPs, which leverage the model's split thresholds to faithfully capture its behavior across all possible feature values.
  Woodelf++ is implemented in pure Python and supports GPU acceleration. On a dataset with 400,000 rows, Woodelf++ computes PDP and Joint-PDP up to 6x faster than the state of the art and up to five orders of magnitude faster than scikit-learn. For Any-Order-PDIVs, the gap is even larger: Woodelf++ computes all interaction values in 5 minutes, while the state of the art is estimated to require over 1,000,000 years.

</details>

Abstract: Extensive research has highlighted the severe threats posed by backdoor attacks to deep reinforcement learning (DRL). Despite their effectiveness in mitigating plasticity loss, the impact of these interventions on DRL backdoor vulnerabilities remains underexplored, and this lack of systematic investigation poses risks in practical DRL deployments. We find that only one intervention (i.e., SAM) exacerbates backdoor threats, while other interventions mitigate them. ### [198] [Silent Collapse in Recursive Learning Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14588)
*Zhipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出并揭示了递归训练模型中存在“沉默崩溃”现象，即模型在传统指标看似稳定时已发生内部退化。为此，作者开发了MTR框架，利用模型内部统计指标的前兆特征，在无需原始数据的情况下实现了对模型退化的早期预警与主动干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归学习在现代大模型训练中日益普及，但传统的性能指标（如损失、准确率）无法在模型发生不可逆的内部退化（即“沉默崩溃”）之前及时捕捉到风险，亟需一种能够早期预警并防止模型自我退化的机制。

Method: 研究者通过追踪递归模型在训练过程中的预测熵、表示多样性和尾部覆盖率等统计指标，识别出模型在性能退化前的三个前兆特征，并构建了MTR（监控-信任-调节）框架，通过动态调节学习强度来实现对模型递归退化的主动干预。

Result: 研究表明，“沉默崩溃”在标准评估指标恶化前表现出明显的轨迹级前兆（锚熵收缩、表示漂移冻结、尾部覆盖率侵蚀）。实验证明，MTR框架能够作为一种轻量级的元认知循环，在无需访问原始数据的情况下，有效识别潜在风险并阻止模型崩溃。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了递归模型训练中普遍存在的“沉默崩溃”现象，并通过提出的MTR框架，证明了在无需原始数据的前提下，通过监控内部统计指标的演变，可以有效预警并防止模型性能的长期退化。

Abstract: Recursive learning -- where models are trained on data generated by previous versions of themselves -- is increasingly common in large language models, autonomous agents, and self-supervised systems. However, standard performance metrics (loss, perplexity, accuracy) often fail to detect internal degradation before it becomes irreversible. Here we identify a phenomenon we call silent collapse: under broad recursive conditions, model internal distributions -- predictive entropy, representational diversity, and tail coverage -- progressively contract even as conventional metrics appear stable or improving.
  We discover that silent collapse is not abrupt. Its onset is reliably preceded by three trajectory-level precursors: (1) contraction of anchor entropy, (2) freezing of representation drift, and (3) erosion of tail coverage. These signals manifest multiple generations before any degradation in standard validation metrics, enabling early warning.
  Based on these precursors, we propose the MTR (Monitor--Trust--Regulator) framework, a lightweight metacognitive loop that monitors trajectory statistics, estimates a slow-timescale trust variable, and adaptively modulates the effective learning intensity. MTR provides early warning and actively prevents silent collapse without requiring access to pristine real data -- a critical advantage when original data is unavailable, contaminated, or private.

### [199] [Forgetting That Sticks: Quantization-Permanent Unlearning via Circuit Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15138)
*Saisab Sadhu,Pratinav Seth,Vinay Kumar Sankarapu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型遗忘在量化压缩后会“失效”的问题，本文提出了MANSU框架，通过确保遗忘更新幅度超过量化阈值并利用因果电路定位，实现了在量化模型中稳健且彻底的知识擦除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘评估忽略了量化（Quantization）对模型行为的影响。研究发现，传统的遗忘方法在4-bit量化后会出现“遗忘失效”或“保持能力退化”的现象，其根源在于遗忘更新幅度过小，无法突破量化区间的限制，导致遗忘行为在压缩后被“反转”。

Method: 提出了一种名为MANSU（机制对齐零空间遗忘）的方法，核心包括三个步骤：1. 利用因果电路归因确定最小遗忘子图；2. 进行电路受限的零空间投影并引入对齐Fisher保持约束；3. 设置参数级的幅度阈值以强制保证遗忘更新跨越量化边界。此外，引入了电路归因散度（CAD）指标来评估结构性擦除。

Result: MANSU在多个模型家族和危险评估基准上表现优异，是首个同时满足有效遗忘、知识保持、量化稳健性和结构擦除的方法。相比之下，传统的基于梯度的遗忘方法在量化后会出现显著的精度恢复，即遗忘失效。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了现有机器遗忘方法在量化模型上的脆弱性，并提出了MANSU框架。通过机制化归因分析与稀疏约束，MANSU不仅实现了模型权重的结构性擦除，还确保了遗忘效果在量化压缩后的稳健性，为可信大模型的部署提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Standard unlearning evaluations measure behavioral suppression in full precision, immediately after training, despite every deployed language model being quantized first. Recent work has shown that 4-bit post-training quantization can reverse machine unlearning; we show this is not a tuning artefact but a systematic dual failure: gradient-based methods that achieve meaningful forgetting lose it under compression, while methods that survive quantization barely change the model. Both failures trace to the same root cause: across all baselines, per-parameter updates lie 47-828x below the NF4 quantization bin width; updates diffused across billions of parameters cannot clear quantization bin boundaries, a consequence we formalize as a sparsity-permanence tradeoff. We present MANSU (Mechanistic-Aligned Null-Space Unlearning), which resolves both modes by combining causal circuit attribution to isolate the minimal forget-set subgraph, circuit-restricted null-space projection with a diagonal-Fisher retain bound, and a per-parameter magnitude floor guaranteeing quantization survival by construction. We additionally introduce Circuit Attribution Divergence (CAD), a mechanistic verification metric distinguishing structural erasure from behavioral suppression, a distinction existing metrics cannot make. Across multiple model families and hazard benchmarks, MANSU is the first method to jointly satisfy all four properties with margin on each (meaningful forgetting, retain preservation, non-positive PTQ gap, and structural erasure), while gradient-based baselines recover up to +0.05 accuracy under compression.

### [200] [Fast Rates for Inverse Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14599)
*Andreas Schlaginhaufen,Maryam Kamgarpour*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过数学证明揭示了熵正则化Min-Max-IRL与极大似然估计的紧密联系，并利用伪自相容性证明了该方法在一般环境下可达到$\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$的最优统计收敛率，且无需额外的环境探索假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的逆强化学习（IRL）算法在理论分析上通常依赖于强假设（如覆盖假设或特定的环境限制），且对于线性奖励类在更一般的Borel状态和动作空间下的统计性质研究不足。本文旨在建立严谨的结构性与统计学框架，以解决IRL在模型误设和缺乏探索假设下的收敛性问题。

Method: 1. 利用伪自相容性（pseudo-self-concordance）分析Min-Max-IRL损失函数的性质；2. 推导软最优价值函数（soft-optimal value function）关于奖励参数的导数；3. 运用统计学习理论分析轨迹级KL散度和参数估计误差的收敛率。

Result: 1. 证明了Min-Max-IRL与MLE在总体水平上的等价性，以及在确定性动力学下的经验等价性；2. 在专家轨迹数$n$趋于无穷时，证明了参数估计误差和KL散度均以$\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$的快收敛速度趋于零；3. 将奖励可辨识性结果推广至一般的Borel空间。

Conclusion: 本文证明了在Borel空间和线性奖励函数类下，熵正则化Min-Max-IRL与极大似然估计（MLE）在结构上的等价性。此外，通过利用损失函数的伪自相容性（pseudo-self-concordance），证明了该算法在专家轨迹数量$n$下的统计收敛速度达到了最优的$\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$，且该结果在模型误设及无需探索假设下依然成立。

Abstract: We establish novel structural and statistical results for entropy-regularized min-max inverse reinforcement learning (Min-Max-IRL) with linear reward classes in finite-horizon MDPs with Borel state and action spaces. On the structural side, we show that maximum likelihood estimation (MLE) and Min-Max-IRL are equivalent at the population level, and at the empirical level under deterministic dynamics. On the statistical side, exploiting pseudo-self-concordance of the Min-Max-IRL loss, we prove that both the trajectory-level KL divergence and the squared parameter error in the Hessian norm decay at the fast rate $\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$, where $n$ is the number of expert trajectories. Our guarantees apply under misspecification and require no exploration assumptions. We further extend reward-identifiability results to general Borel spaces and derive novel results on the derivatives of the soft-optimal value function with respect to reward parameters.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a central paradigm for post-training LLM agents, yet its trajectory-level reward signal provides only coarse supervision for long-horizon interaction. On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) complements RL by introducing dense token-level guidance from a teacher branch augmented with privileged context. However, transferring OPSD to multi-turn agents proves problematic: compounding multi-turn instability destabilizes supervision, while skill-conditioned privileged guidance requires asymmetric treatment for negative teacher rejections may arise from imperfect skills retrieval or utilization. We introduce SDAR (Self-Distilled Agentic Reinforcement Learning), which treats OPSD as a gated auxiliary objective while keeping RL as the primary optimization backbone. SDAR maps detached token-level signals into a sigmoid gate, strengthening distillation on teacher-endorsed positive-gap tokens and softly attenuating negative teacher rejections. Across the Qwen2.5 and Qwen3 families on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Search-QA, SDAR substantially improves over GRPO (+9.4% on ALFWorld, +7.0% on Search-QA, +10.2% on WebShop-Acc), avoids the instability of naive GRPO+OPSD, and consistently outperforms hybrid RL--OPSD baselines across model scales.

### [202] [An Amortized Efficiency Threshold for Comparing Neural and Heuristic Solvers in Combinatorial Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14624)
*Sohaib Afifi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种衡量神经组合优化求解器能源效率的新框架（AET），证明了只要部署规模足够大，神经求解器在总能源消耗上可以显著优于传统启发式算法，从而推翻了“神经求解器因训练昂贵而必然低效”的常见观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了“摊销效率阈值（AET）”框架，用于对比神经求解器与CPU元启发式算法在特定部署规模下的总能源或碳排放。通过在多任务车辆路径规划问题（MTVRP）上进行实证，测量了两种求解器在不同部署量下的累积能源比率及交叉点（盈亏平衡点）。

Result: 在MTVRP环境（n=20）的实验中，测量得到的AET交叉点约为1.58 × 10^5次部署。当单次推断性能优于启发式算法时，其累积能源比率趋向于一个小于1的常数（实测为0.41），证明了在达到一定部署规模后，神经求解器在总能源成本上具有优势。

Conclusion: 本文论证了针对神经组合优化求解器的“能效低下”论点在未考虑部署规模时存在逻辑缺陷。通过引入AET框架，研究表明当部署规模足够大时，神经求解器在总能源消耗上可以优于传统启发式算法。研究为评估AI模型的实际环境可持续性提供了科学的方法论。

Abstract: A common critique of neural combinatorial-optimization solvers is that they are less energy-efficient than CPU metaheuristics, given the operational energy cost of training them on GPUs. This paper examines the inferential step from "training is expensive" to "neural solvers are net-inefficient", which is where the critique actually goes wrong. Training the network costs a large fixed amount of GPU energy; running the metaheuristic costs a small amount of CPU energy on every instance, repeated as long as the solver is deployed. The two are not commensurable until a deployment volume is fixed. We define the Amortized Efficiency Threshold (AET) as the deployment volume above which a neural solver breaks even with a heuristic baseline in total energy or carbon, under an explicit constraint on solution quality. We show that the cumulative-energy ratio between the two solvers tends to a constant strictly below one whenever the network wins per-instance, and that this limit does not depend on how the training cost was measured. An embodied-carbon term amortizes hardware fabrication symmetrically on both sides. We instantiate the framework on the Multi-Task VRP (MTVRP) environment at n=20 customers across 19 problem variants and five training seeds, with HGS via PyVRP as the heuristic baseline. The measured crossover sits near $1.58 \times 10^5$ deployed instances; the per-instance ratio is 0.41, reflecting the moderate size of the instances tested. The contribution is the framework, the open instrumentation, and the measurement protocol; structural convergence of the ratio at larger problem sizes is left to future empirical work.

### [203] [FutureSim: Replaying World Events to Evaluate Adaptive Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15188)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 FutureSim 基准，旨在测试 AI 智能体对真实世界未来事件的预测与适应能力。测试结果显示，当前顶尖 AI 模型在处理动态环境和长时程预测方面仍存在显著短板，准确率较低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 AI 智能体被部署在动态且开放的环境中，现有的评估方法难以衡量智能体处理新信息及长时程预测的能力。研究者希望通过模拟真实世界事件演进的路径，定量评估智能体在面对未知未来时的预测水平与推理适应性。

Method: 提出了 FutureSim 仿真框架。该框架通过按时间顺序重播真实世界事件（如新闻动态和事件结果），要求 AI 智能体在已知知识截止日期之后，针对未来三个月内发生的世界事件进行预测和推理，从而评估其动态环境下的适应能力。

Result: 评估结果显示，现有的前沿 AI 智能体在 FutureSim 上的表现差距显著，最佳智能体的准确率仅为 25%，甚至许多模型的 Brier 技巧得分低于随机猜测。实验证实该基准能有效揭示智能体在长视距、测试时适应及推理能力上的不足。

Conclusion: FutureSim 为评估 AI 智能体在开放世界中的长期预测与适应能力提供了一个切实可行的基准。该研究指出，当前顶尖智能体在处理实时、动态的真实世界信息时能力有限，未来需要针对长时程测试时适应、检索、记忆和不确定性推理等方向进行深入研究。

Abstract: AI agents are being increasingly deployed in dynamic, open-ended environments that require adapting to new information as it arrives. To efficiently measure this capability for realistic use-cases, we propose building grounded simulations that replay real-world events in the order they occurred. We build FutureSim, where agents forecast world events beyond their knowledge cutoff while interacting with a chronological replay of the world: real news articles arriving and questions resolving over the simulated period. We evaluate frontier agents in their native harness, testing their ability to predict world events over a three-month period from January to March 2026. FutureSim reveals a clear separation in their capabilities, with the best agent's accuracy being 25%, and many having worse Brier skill score than making no prediction at all. Through careful ablations, we show how FutureSim offers a realistic setting to study emerging research directions like long-horizon test-time adaptation, search, memory, and reasoning about uncertainty. Overall, we hope our benchmark design paves the way to measure AI progress on open-ended adaptation spanning long time-horizons in the real world.

### [204] [Unbiased and Second-Order-Free Training for High-Dimensional PDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14643)
*Jaemin Seo,Surin Lee,Jae Yong Lee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种新的训练框架，通过对EM离散化诱导的损失偏差进行严谨的数学分析，消除了这种偏差，且该方法保留了BSDE求解器无需计算二阶空间导数（即无二阶导数）的计算优势。

Result: 实验表明，该新框架在处理高维偏微分方程时，能够有效解决EM方案带来的偏差问题，实现了无偏估计，同时维持了算法在计算开销方面的显著优势。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论分析揭示了欧拉-丸山（EM）离散化在求解BSDE时产生损失偏差的本质原因，并成功提出了一种无需计算二阶导数的无偏训练框架，在保持计算效率的同时提升了求解高维偏微分方程的准确性。

Abstract: Deep learning methods based on backward stochastic differential equations (BSDEs) have emerged as competitive alternatives to physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) for solving high-dimensional partial differential equations (PDEs). By leveraging probabilistic representations, BSDE approaches can avoid the curse of dimensionality and often admit second-order-free training objectives that do not require explicit Hessian evaluations. It has recently been established that the commonly used Euler-Maruyama (EM) time discretization induces an intrinsic bias in BSDE training losses. While high-order schemes such as Heun can fully eliminate this bias, such schemes re-introduce second-order spatial derivatives and incur substantial computational overhead. In this work, we provide a principled analysis of EM-induced loss bias and propose an unbiased, second-order-free training framework that preserves the computational advantages of BSDE methods. Our code is available at https://github.com/seojaemin22/Un-EM-BSDE.

### [205] [Slower Generalization, Faster Memorization: A Sweet Spot in Algorithmic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14659)
*Shin So,Kyelim Lee,Albert No*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了“数据越多越好”的直觉，指出在Needleman-Wunsch等结构化任务中，存在一个最优数据集规模，超出该规模反而会增加模型达到泛化收敛所需的训练步数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的“Grokking（顿悟）”理论认为，一旦数据量足够识别底层规则，增加数据应能加速泛化收敛。该研究旨在验证这一直觉在复杂结构化输出任务中是否成立，并探究数据规模对学习过程的具体影响机制。

Method: 通过受控的结构化输出任务（Needleman-Wunsch矩阵生成），对比不同数据集大小对Transformer模型训练效率及泛化能力的影响，并将其与乘法任务基线进行对比实验，以此探究数据量对模型学习规则与记忆拟合的不同影响。

Result: 在Needleman-Wunsch任务中发现存在数据规模的“甜点”：模型在中间规模数据集上达到最高验证准确率的速度最快。超过此规模后，尽管模型仍能泛化，但需要更多的梯度更新。这一现象在乘法基线任务中未出现，证明了该特征与任务的结构化性质有关。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了“数据量并非越多越好”的现象，证明了在某些结构化输出任务中，存在一个能够实现泛化收敛的最优数据量区间（甜点），超过该区间反而会拖慢模型收敛速度。这表明学习规则与完成精确拟合之间存在解耦，挑战了传统的简单缩放直觉。

Abstract: Critical-data-size accounts of grokking suggest a natural post-threshold intuition: once training data is sufficient to identify the underlying rule, additional data should accelerate validation convergence. We show that this intuition can fail in a controlled structured-output task. In Needleman--Wunsch (NW) matrix generation, small Transformers reach high validation exact-match accuracy fastest at an intermediate dataset size, not at the largest one. Past this dataset-size sweet spot, generalization remains achievable but requires more gradient updates. Conversely, in the regime where partial validation competence first appears, larger datasets can require fewer updates to reach high training accuracy, suggesting that emerging rule structure can accelerate fitting beyond example-wise memorization. A multiplication baseline does not show the same post-threshold slowdown. These results separate the critical data size for the onset of generalization from the dataset size that optimizes update-based convergence, and identify structured-output tasks where learning the rule and completing exact-fitting can diverge.
